内外債整委會 1

宋子文提出報告書

（南京）　内外債整理委員會、六日上午十時、在國府舉行會議、到委員長王寵惠·委員王正廷·王伯羣·孫科·宋子文·孔祥熙、主席王寵惠、討論、（一）宋子文提出報告書、叙述十八年度整理内外債經過、及决定整理辦法案、决議、呈送政府核閱後公布、（二）定十三日在國府繼續會議、據該會某委員談、刻因内債團尚未整個成立、外債團之調查、亦未完全送到、故現時進行、仍爲審查事項、關於本會聘請各委員之資格己確定、一·與職權有關者、二·專家、三·銀行界、現己聘就三十餘人、將來大會時、均將出席、又謂對内外債之整理、係採平等辦法、并無輕重厚薄之分、（六日專電）

胡病勢昨轉佳 2

孫科等擬接胡入城調養

（南京）戴季陶談、胡漢民到湯山後、身體不適、二日胡之女公子木蘭、隨帶女僕、前往視疾、三日請鐵部鄧眞德醫官往診、是晚、鄧即往湯山、四日鄧回京取藥、據云、胡係患後腦神經病、兼發痔疾、及胃腸不適、五日晨、鄧打電話、謂胡昨晚頭暈、熱度稍高、午後三時余與孫科先往慰問、蔣派劉瑞恒診視、見胡温度脈搏己如常、惟血壓頗高、須絶對靜養、並服易消化之滋養品、六日晨、鄧回京云、昨晚安眠、較前兩作爲佳、食牛肉汁麥粉、狀均良好、又劉瑞恒謂、胡之病狀、五日下午、熱度九十九、脈搏八十、漸復常態、但頭胃兩部、稍有疼痛、測其血壓、高至二百、當係操勞過度所致、小便現正化騐、其他尚無重要病象、六日上午、又往診視一次、並無異狀、惟血壓過高、亟應長期靜養、（六日專電）

（南京）聞孫科·孔祥熙等、以胡漢民臥病湯山、診視不便、鐵部後面孫之私邸、空氣清暢、擬接胡入城、至彼處調養、（六日專電）

印度非武力之成功 33

非武力之抵抗。其威權甚武力。其苦痛之加於對方者較無論任何力量爲尤大而非武力抵抗之諸辦法中。更以抵貨一事爲最有力故自印度實行非武力抵抗後、英國商業之受其影響實非淺鮮。今一旦得有撤銷之機會商業可由此活動。英工黨與自由黨及一般商民固表示滿意即其他反對政府之黨。雖問有以讓步過甚責備政府。但鑒於商業之不能不設法維持故亦無猛烈之攻擊。是可見非武力運動效力之大也。

且印人非武力運動之影響。不僅及於英國而己。昨華盛頓電謂商界對於印

督與甘地談判之成功。甚爲欣慰。預料此良好影響及於美商業並信有益於美國與墨西哥之銀礦業。今日紐約電亦謂、市塲銀價較昨日高漲四分之一半因印度局勢現己轉佳之故。又可知印度問題。關係世界商業金融之大與其影響之捷矣、夫以今日商業之不振。銀價之低跌。爲世界各國共感之苦痛原因又甚複雜。印度問題之所得挽回者。固其微之又微然因其機之動。凡與金融商業有關之各方面各問題各種人心之覺悟。皆趨向於圜之一途。事事得順利之解决。則可危可懼之今年。或即轉爲可慶可喜之今年歟

印督與甘地恊定原文發表 57

非武力反抗有效終止

抵貨不復爲政治工具

紐約銀市趨漲風

▲路透社五日新德里電　印督與甘地間協定原文○現己用一種官塲文告正式發表、除己宣佈之條欵外、此項文告並聲明依照一月九日英相之允許、行將設法使全印大會代表參加日後關於憲法改善計劃、如圓桌會議所規劃者之討論、又謂外貨之抵制、大抵對英貨而施以發生政治目的之壓力、故議定非武力反抗之終止、含有切實終止抵制英貨、不再以此爲政治工具之意、至於推銷印貨以代非印貨之方法、或取締烈酒與藥物銷費之方法、除不出普通法律所許之範圍者外、未可採用糾察、如糾察在任何地方形成侵犯、則須停止之、甘地曾主張公開調查鬧事警察行爲、但甘地旣知此事有種種困難、或將礙及和平之恢復、故允不堅持、前己没收之産業、除原業主頑抗拒繳地稅與其他捐稅者外、皆須發還、惟不動産己售與第三方面者、則就政府而言、此種交易莫可變更、但任何人皆可求法律上之救濟、凡因自行辭職而空出之位置、如己有人補充、則政府未能恢復前人之原職、惟其他辭職事件、各地方政府當以寛大之精神考慮、末稱、如全印大會不能履行此項協定之義務、則政府得採行任何必要方法、以保護公共而維持法紀云、

▲路透社五日倫敦電　印度事務部大臣邊恩今日在下院宣讀新德里發表之文告、並說明非武力反抗之有效的終止、即各種活動凡以採用各種方法促進反抗爲目的者、如反抗土地法·拒絶納稅發報紙提倡反抗運動·文武官員反對政府·或離棄職守等運動、一律有效的終止之意、

▲路透社六日倫敦電　印督與甘地談話之結果、甚爲官塲所滿意、保守黨雖不如工當與自由黨之表示欣快、但對於所議定之辦法、大都無間言也、報紙雖有數家覺此協定難以忍受、但多數評論措詞頗合情理、一般人注意點在抵制之撤銷、與英商業因此而受之效果、

▲美聨社五日紐約電　今日市塲銀價漲高、半因印度局勢現己轉佳之故、銀價收盤爲二七又八分之七、較昨收盤價高四分之一、

廣州通信、十九路總指揮蔣光鼐、日前疊接前方將領聨電、催請入贛主持督師剿匪、當時蔣氏以剿匪事宜、尚待陳濟棠返省磋商、故未出發、但自接陳濟棠南返日期後、即决定於三月一日啓程入贛、查陳濟棠於上月二十八日返抵廣州、蔣氏是日與陳磋商妥洽後、即於當晚飭屬摒擋行裝、及飭醫愈官兵準備、並請省府函飭廣韶路局長劉鞠可、預備花車一輛、三等車六輛、輜重車八輛應用、今日上午六時、廣韶路局即如數掛車、在黄沙站候用、七時許、該部醫愈士兵約千餘人、列隊到站登車、各軍實行李、則用車運到、分儎輜重車中、直至九時二十分方始完竣、九時五十分、蔣氏即偕夫人及女公子等乘車抵站、斯時軍樂齊奏、蔣氏携同夫人下車、步上月台、與各歡送者一一握手爲禮、隨到站長室休息候車、愚因投剌訪問、與蔣氏作如下之談話、（問）總指揮現在赴北江乎、蔣（答）然、（問）行程能見告否、（答）先抵韶關、然後取道陸路、經南雄大庾、直往贛州、（問）預計若干日方能到贛州、（答）因沿途尚有别事、日期不能預定、（問）抵贛州後尚往興國會蔡師長否、（答）抵步時再定、（問）往南昌會何主任應欽否、（答）尚未定、（問）贛省共匪踪、現在何處、（答）匪踪飄忽、出没無常、大約仍在雩都等地、（問）總指揮抵贛後、其剿匪步驟能否見告、（答）先將各部隊集中、即施行向匪總攻擊、至計劃則須請命何主任、（問）總指揮之意、若干時日方能將匪肅清、（答）因匪黨拼命　扎、肅清之時期、很難固定、惟積極計劃圍剿、希望於最短期内辦到、以安民衆、（問）蔡師長現在何處、（答）仍在興國行營主持、（問）今晨隨同總指揮出發部隊有若干、（答）有醫愈士兵約兩營、（問）隨行職員有幾位、（答）有參謀吳典等十餘人、（問）黄延禎旅長偕同乘車返韶乎、（答）黄旅長因任務完竣、故約同今晨乘車返韶、（問）總指揮抵韶關逗留否、（答）或不逗留、談至此、適李揚敬黄延禎等與蔣氏談論要務、愚遂辭出、十時二十分、專車己由黄沙站開抵西村、蔣氏偕黄延禎及職員衞弁等登車、十時三十分、汽笛三聲、車遂啓行、各歡送者亦分乘汽車而散、（三月一日）

▲平漢交通梗塞二日下午二時、由漢開平之特别快車、行至廣水時、己在夜問、即有探報、謂李家寨新店等處發現匪共萬餘人騷擾、不能前進、當即在廣水候至三四時之久、仍未得北面之新店車站電告、爲安全旅客起見、即折回漢口、於三日午後二時、回抵大智門車站、至路局損失、據調查當匪竄至後、新店車站機車二輛、爲匪搗毀、站内一切器具、亦被毀盡、沿途廣水至柳林段電桿、折斷者四十餘根、鐵軌毀斷甚多、損失約計萬餘元左右、現平漢北上車暫時行至廣水爲終點、（三月四日）

▲决發輔幣劵五十萬元

長沙通信、湖南省銀行、係魯滌平任省府主席時所設、由省庫撥一百萬元爲基金、並未發行紙幣、何鍵繼任後、因統稅收入暢旺、又加撥基金五十萬元、總共該行資本一百五十萬元、兩年以來、營業頗有贏餘、自去年六月張桂軍攻陷長沙、第四路軍因軍費緊急、向省銀行提用基金六十萬元、尚未歸還、而共匪彭德懷又於七月二十七日竄陷長沙、何鍵乃將該行所存欵項、全數提去、作爲軍費、計該行資本一百五十萬元、被政府提去五分之四、其餘五分之一、因放在商家、尚未到期、故得保存、迨去年八月長沙收復後、該行即未正式復業、半年以來、祇收不放、截至現在、己將放在商家之欵約三十萬元、陸續收回、至於政府提去之基金、因財政困難、尚未撥還分文、現實際上該行資本己不到五十萬元、近何鍵爲活潑市面調劑金融起見、决定用該行名義發行紙幣、因中央限制各省銀行不准發行一元以上之鈔票、故决定發行輔幣劵、分一角二角五角三種、在長沙湘鄂印刷局印製、總額暫定五十萬元、分兩期發出、第一次發行二十萬元、十足現金準備、俟有信用後、再發三十萬元、即用保證準備、所有票幣、均己印製完竣、定三月十日起開始發行、其發行章程與準備金檢查章程、均己公布、現在湘省市面上行使輔幣劵、計有四種、（一）上海中國銀行輔幣劵、（二）湖北省銀行輔幣劵、（三）湖南電燈公司發行之當一二三角輔幣劵、（四）湖南和豐火柴公司發行之當一二五角輔幣劵、前兩項數目不多、後兩項充斥全省市面、約有四十萬元、聞省府决定俟湖南省銀行輔幣劵發行後、對於該兩公司發行之輔幣劵、將勒令一律收回、以免影響市面、（三月四日）

天津號滯留濟南 76

▲右翼油管滲漏

濟南通信、中國航空公司作滬平試航、該公司監察兼機航組副主任聶開一等四人、於二日乘天津號飛機、由徐州飛到濟南、昨晚天津代理市長張啓芳來電、謂天津飛機塲可以降落、於是天津號决定飛往天津、今日（四日）上午九點三十分、由張莊飛機塲上昇飛出、在城内空中盤旋一週、即循津浦北飛、詎於九點五十分又飛回張莊降下、愚適在該處、即訪聶開一、據談今晨出發後、在城内空中高至二千尺、天空極爲清朗、及飛過黄河上、空中大霧瀰漫、遂降低至八百尺、繼續北飛、速度亦略减小、飛至桑梓店、忽發見右翼有白色冰　狀物、在上海出發時、本己發見右翼油管滲油、但不碍飛行、至此則不敢冐險、故飛回檢查、現己騐得右翼油管之一、滲滴較鉅、左翼之二、尚可勉强、惟必需修理、始能飛行、目下所最感困難者、在濟恐不能修理、聶談至此、遂問愚大槐樹鐵路工廠有熟人否、請爲介紹、愚以鐵路工廠副廠長秦文範告、聶遂派械機員于湧泉、（昨誤爲于飛泉）偕愚前往、與秦副廠長晤談後、仍無辦法、因油管係鋼種（按即鋁）製、須用養氣銲、（按即氯氣銲）鐵路工廠只有電氣銲、無濟於事、嗣由秦副廠長介紹陸大鐵工廠有養氣銲、及由電話中詢問、則己損壞、不能應用、至此修理己完全失望、聶遂一面電天津報告、一面電滬、請派人持銲器來濟修理、預計航空公司派人、至六日晚始能隨平浦車到濟、如修理得手、亦須於七日下午始能飛出、今日下午、聶又偕飛機師機械員等、在張莊飛機塲試飛、將右翼左翼之裂管塞住、僅由其餘之二管出油、試飛十五分鐘、仍即降下、據聶談試飛結果尚佳、但由濟飛津、須費時一小時半、僅由兩管供油、能否敷用、尚無把握、明早當再試飛一次、如有把握、即飛往天津、否則須俟修理以後云、（三月四日）

鄂省委方陳就職 78

▲何成濬何奇陽監誓

漢口通信、湖北省政府建設廳廳長方達智·委員陳光組·於二日上午十時、舉行宣誓就職典禮、到中央及行政院監誓委員何成濬·國府監誓委員何奇陽·民政廳長吳醒亞·財政廳長張貫時·教育廳長黄建中·漢口市長劉文島等、由何成濬主席、行禮後、方陳兩氏宣讀誓詞、即由中央監誓委員何成濬致訓詞、略謂·今日方廳長陳委員同時舉行就職典禮、兄弟奉中央黨部及行政院電令監誓、在方陳兩同志能力和學識、大家盡都知道、希望自今以後、遵照誓詞、切實做去、誓詞裏面、概括起來、不外數點、一是忠誠、一是廉潔、一是勤愼、而忠誠的忠字、即是總理訓示我們忠孝仁愛信義和平的忠、總理對此八字、將忠字列在第一、是狠有意義、因爲忠字的工夫能做到、則其餘七字、也不難做到、在政府辦事人員、欲盡忠心及努力於本職、則須對於匪共未清·必思有以清之、貪污未除·必思有以除之、建設工作尚未完成·必思有以成之、推而至於民衆之衣食住行各問題、有尚未解决者、必思有以解决之、果能如此、自然勤愼、自然廉潔、對於總理遺教、亦自不違背、一切訓政工作、尤可順利進行、爲政不在多言、顧力行何如、今後希望方陳兩同志、依照誓詞、切實努力云云、次國府監誓委員何奇陽致訓詞、略謂·陳委員歷次參加北伐、最近輔佐何主席、將唐生智及馮閻諸逆打倒、功績素著、方廳長歷任鐵路局長、學識經騐、兩俱優長、以前本省政治、因省府組織不甚健全、致無成績表現、建設方面、亦無若何樹立、現省政己臻健全、建設事業、又有方廳長切實負責、相信方陳二同志就職後、必有良好表現云云、次陳委員光組致答詞、略謂·光組向學軍旅、政治本非所長、現承國府任命、自當遵照中央及省府一切法令、追隨何主席及各委員之後、努力做去、方廳長答詞謂、達智學識　陋、深虞隕越、此後當追隨何主席及各委員之後、加倍努力、並請在座諸君、隨時賜教云云、禮畢奏樂攝影散會、何主席於散會後、當即分電中央行政院、報告監誓就職經過矣、（三月二日）

此外擬提倡者、計畫按事編印各種農林淺說、散布民間、如植棉之改良、施肥之質量、以及開溝蓄水治田鑿井等事、均分委專員、按照陜西實際情形、斟酌辦理、廣事宣傳、以收宏效、

第七、關於文化者、擬先建設陳列館於西安、凡各國各項機器農具、可爲陜省實用者、均擇要陳列、以資人民仿效、又陳列國内外商品、以資比較摹製、至本省農工物産、亦廣微博收、分類陳列、並逐件說明其用途製造、以引起民衆實業興趣、開辦費擬定十萬元、以後逐漸擴充、其次擬建設氣象台于華山、與國内各大氣象台聨絡、開辦費以五萬元起、逐漸擴充、其次擬推行量雨器于各縣、器由建設廳製造、令各縣購領、

以上三事、本年均須計盡妥當、以備實施、此外有應修復者、一爲臨潼縣之華清公園、一爲西安市之革命紀念公園、華清公園、包有驪山温泉之勝、擬修復以後、並建築旅館一所、以爲遊人憇息之地、共需工費約十萬元、革命紀念公園、地址闊大、完成尚需時日、計畫工費、約需五萬元、以上各種計畫、均陜西目前重要之圖、亦陜民生活必需之事、實則千瘡百孔之陜西、何事不待建設、語云、登高必自卑、行遠必自邇、兹二十年者不過陜西建設實施之發軔、實不敢詞涉張大、蹈空言無補之轍以誤民生也、（完）

教育消息要聞

日本中蟘革命 99

▲足供我國教育界參考

喧擾多年之日本中學制度改革問題、己於本年一月十日由文部省將改正中學校規程公布、四月十日施行、其要點如下、

一·中學校、以依據中學校令的趣旨、於小學校教育上、施以較高程度的道德教育國民教育及生活上有用的普通知能、且勵行體育爲宗旨、特别留意於左列各項、（一）依據教育勅語、使學校教育全體道德教育化、常導學生實踐躬行、更宜留意於國民道德的養成使會得建國的本義與國體的尊嚴、忠孝的大義、鞏固其信仰、（二）努力於養成獨立自主的精神、愛好勤勞的習慣、尊重協力、重視責任的美德、（三）宜專以啓發心力爲旨、使不拘拘於專門學術的體系、而以養成社會生活上適切有用的知能、

二·中學校五年畢業、其學科爲修身、公民科、國語漢文、歷史、地理、外國語、數學、理科、實業、圖畫作業科、體操、第四學年以上的年級、編制第一第二兩種課程、使學生選修其一種、兩種課程的共同基本科目爲修身、公民科、國語漢文、歷史、地理、理科、體操第一種課程、除基本科目外、可增課以國語漢文、外國語數學、理科、圖畫、音樂、内適宜的教科目及實業、第二種課程、除基本科目外、可增課以國語漢文、數學、理科圖畫、音樂中適宜的數科目及外國語、前項規定、從第三學年起、亦可適用但其共同基本科目、爲修身、公民科、國語、漢文、歷史、地理、數學、理科、作業科、體操、第一種可增課以國語漢文、外國語數學、理科、圖畫、音樂中適宜的教科目及實業第一種可增以國語漢文、教學、理科、圖畫音樂中適宜的數科目及外國語、又遇有特别情形、得請求文部省之許、可酌減科目、實業科目課以工業或農業時得缺少作業科、

三·各學年每週教授時數若在第四學年以上分爲第一二種課程編制時、用甲種、表若在第三學年分種編制時、用乙種表、甲號衣中第三學年的音樂、得缺之、缺作業科時、其教授時數、可配以其他科目、實業、作業科、圖畫音樂等的實習、及體操的教授時數·得於甲或一號衣的規定時間外課之、甲號衣或乙號衣以外、每週得於二小時以内課以課程外的指導事項、甲乙兩號表略

四·各學科的教授宜求聨絡以期益益、

五·實業科、授以關於實業的知識技能、使了解實際的生活、養成尊重職業、勤勉力行之風、

實業科、課以農業工業或商業又或適宜分合教授之

六·作業科、以藉重作業、養成學生愛好勤勞的習慣且得日常生活上有用的知能爲主旨、作業科課以園藝工作及其他作業、第三學年以上得課以用器畫爲主的作業、

以上係摘取規程大要至此次改正、着眼於下列數點、（一）注意於思想善導（二）注意於能升學的學生與不能升學的學生、分别編制課程爲甲乙二種、（三）注意於職業教育（四）注意於鄰國語言即中國語言、（五）採用混合教授方法、（六）注意於作業教育（七）於基本科目的外設、增加科目、該科目得選擇之、（八）增加科目的教授時數、使富於彈牲、

自由談

世界小事記

— 海客

▲法國交際塲中有一位著名的女交際家在家裏養着許多猴子。專取它們的毛以作衣裳上滾邊之用

▲據荷蘭一位天文家宣稱。天空中的星。是分作兩路。

展開如水波一樣而彼此相背行動的。

▲英國一位博物家說。水鰻游行極快。計其一生經行之路。每尾平均在六千英里左右。可抵得地球的環行四分之一。

▲美國根德甘州的離婚法中。夫婦離婚的理由、計有十一條之多。性情惡劣不可遏制。與宗教不同。也包含在内。

▲英國白拉頓地方。有一對雙生子。最近舉行九十歳生辰祝典。據說這二人是英吉利全國最老的雙生子。

▲英倫三島。共有養病的區城一百五十處。可以供給種種所需要的氣候。以適合於病者的身體。

▲倫敦向有一種工役。專給人揩抹皮鞋以爲生活的。計有二千餘人。近來因普通的人都講經濟。揩抺皮鞋。都由自己動手。所以這班工役。現己减至四百人。

▲非洲有好幾處地方的土人。流行一種遊戲。用八英尺長的繩子。在一頭打成了一個圈兒。彼此甩擲爲戲。

記客談吳昌碩之寫像 125

— 鄭逸梅

丹靑中有所謂傳神者。蓋以筆墨摹寫人狀貌。而得其精神也。傳神二字。始見於世說。顧長康畫人。或數年不點目睛。人問其故。曰傳神正在阿堵中。世俗傳神。大都矜持呆版。作衣冠端坐之狀。匠氣滿紙。腐惡欲嘔。有名畫家。恥不屑爲。然爲名賢冩照。布園林之景。衣着不加刻畫。飄逸有致者。亦得傳世成品。山隂任頣伯年氏。爲吳昌碩寫像蕉蔭石牀間。昌碩裸裎其體。手揮蒲　。據坐其上。一種閒適之意。盎然溢露於縑輻之中。自屬任氏佳構。昌碩死。其畫集中曾以寫像製珂羅版刋印於其端。去歳。江灣路六三園。開昌碩遺畫展覽會。予固景仰老缶者。且六三園距寓居近。廼往作一度之參觀。任伯年氏所寫之像高張於素壁。筆意蒼秀。與尋常傳神。逈有天壤之别。對之令人想像前輩風流不置。斯畫深印腦幕。己間寒暑。客有稔熟昌碩生平者謂任氏之寫像初非寫昌碩之像也。其像短軀而勝。恰與昌碩相稱。昌碩得之。剜去其頭面、倩人圖己容。而付諸裝池。居然補綴熨貼。一如無縫天衣。諺有所謂改頭换面者。昌碩竟猶獪實行之。客之所述。未知果確否。但事頗趣雋。不妨誌之。爲關心畫苑者一解頣也。

大連女學生選夫標準之測騐 126

— 綠珠

大連日文報載云。大連之女學校。首推彌生高等女學校。該校對於畢業生之出路等問題。一向頗爲注意。最近施行選夫標準之測騐。尤爲轟動一時。本届春季畢業生。計共一百八十七名。該校長爲欲明悉彼等對於將來結婚之希望。印就一種表格。區分資格職業等數欄。發給各畢業生塡注。藉以了解各畢業生對於選擇夫婿之態度。結果。則願夫婿爲公司職員者。居一百一十票。一般有薪給者十票。爲教師者十八票。爲實業家者爲二十五票。爲官吏者祇十三票。其他願夫婿爲軍人者共八票。其中六票。係願夫婿爲從事陸軍者二票。餘則希望從事海軍。希望擇政治家爲夫婿者四票。希望擇藝術家爲夫婿者亦只二票。以醫師爲理想中之夫婿者。計九票。至於希望將來之夫婿從事農業者及自由職業者。各僅一票。綜此一百八十七票中塡明夫婿之教育程度。希望中等學校以上畢業者。約居百分之五十。注明須要大學畢業者。不過二十有二人。最有趣者。即此一百八十七票中。注明對飲酒絶對反對者。居一百五十餘票之多。而對於吸烟問題。則幾乎全部采取寛大之態度。又據該校校長之披露。謂願夫婿爲公司職員者之一百十票中。大半注明以南滿鐵道從事員爲最滿意。蓋因南滿鐵道之從事者。大率能得優厚薪給之故耳。

初春小食譜 127

— 楊一笑

▲蝦油蒸小黄魚取小黄魚一　尾。洗淨後加蝦油兩匙。清鹽一撮。置飯鑊上蒸熟。鮮而可口。

▲韮芽拌蟹糊皮　虱蟹和鴨蛋。攤成蟹糊皮一張。切爲狹長薄片。以韮芽拦之。再加醋醬油少許。鮮美絶倫。

▲螺絲肉炒蝦仁螺螄同鮮蝦去殼後。入猪油熱鑊内。略加好醬油。炒二三炒即止。鮮而且嫩。

▲竹徇藏鮮肉漿　竹箰去殼。剖開取鮮肉斬爲漿。藏之笱中。入鑊内。加醬油紅燒。燒熟後再加木耳。厥味腴美異常。

誌埃及古代甲蟲佩印 128

— 鄒今適

元旦日。余偕戈妹與劉君範猷伉儷。參觀明復圖書館書版展覽。其中宋元明清精槧精鈔本。不下數百種。分類陳列。萃海内藏家秘本於一堂。以供衆覽。非徒一時之快事。亦數千年來未有之盛舉。洵可樂也。外此若殷墟甲骨。齊魯封泥。秦漢銅印。唐人寫經。雷峰藏經。均爲人間希世秘寳。古色古香。盈溢一室。其尤可奇異者。厥爲張天方氏所莊埃及古代甲蟲佩印。實爲見所未見。聞所未聞者。印形皆椭圓。大者如拇指。小僅如瓜仁。背鏤象甲蟲。故以爲名。腹刻文字。中有小孔。蓋爲貫索之處。以爲佩。體色翠綠。驟視之。宛然一甲蟲也。顧余嗜古成癖。一見而奇。奇而狂喜。曰。符壐之用。豈獨吾國歟。惜張氏不在。不得面質。越月餘。往訪老友曹禮吾君於曁大。遂得禮吾之介。謁天方先生。余即以求示古印爲請。時值先生家居養疴。即慨然而起。出印以示。殷殷垂教。印計四十五鈕。（有兩印無字）其質或石或匋。古色爛斑。殆數千年前物。爲先生留法時所得。每即之值。約四五元。非特中土未之前有。即外國藏家亦所罕觀。殊爲珍秘。考其文字率皆吉語或神道。蓋用佩於胸前。可以祓除不祥之意。字體奇古精妙。自有别緻。有數字一印。或一字一印。章法匀宜。細巧入微。有日月山川之象。有如裸女而起舞。或趺坐而鼓琴。有如執轡而立。或携杖而行。埃人造字之源。於此可見。余摩挲良久。愛不忍釋。乃手爲鈐拓。以印過小。摘印爲難。盡半日始成四十三紙。而指痛己不堪矣。印畢。稍事休息。張氏復出示所藏埃及瓷石古器數十事。無不精美可喜。張氏工詩文。又邃於考古。故所聚多而且精。所作考古學一卷。及南邨一集見貽。乃興辭而别。歸而援筆記其顚末。以告海内好古君子。

搦象補聞 129

— 清癯

余前「志手搦之肖象」一則刋出後。承朋好見告。謂嘉邑猶有前輩顧志偉顧劍舟兩先生之遺象、亦係一時所塐。至今完好如初。而余未之獲睹。殊爲遺憾。

越昨葛君劍潭又謂現在搦象之名手。尚有其人。渠友某君在滬。曾搦伉儷二象。時在前年春仲。其塐者則倩自蘇之光福鄉。而其名己佚。但憶姓鄭。且不易得其許可。必輾轉間接促其駕。始得惠臨一試其技。至則又未可僅以藝人待之。必誠必虔。有若上賓。而其工作。與人對坐。輙在几下爲之。故人始終不知其如何。其象之成。歷時非至月餘不可。面貎未竣。固不許出示。衣摺具矣。而履鳥未完。則仍秘不稍露、迨見。則栩栩欲動。無論知與不知。皆能識其人而指其名也。其技之神。有如是者。并云代價亦甚鉅。每搦一象。須近百圓。而供飲憇息之所需。猶不計焉、

據上所述。與余前志之事實略同。而時間相違。殆别有其人。而同具斯詣者。唯同爲蘇人。雖皆不知其名。吾謂必有識其。人者。或者其一派之嫡傳。爲其後裔。故能後先輝映於世。余雅好藝事。此尤品之絶作者。不得不一再述之。亦欲冀世之博聞者。有以廣之焉。

煮魚重生記 130

— 吳吉人

去冬嚴寒。爲南中三十年來所未有。不佞偕内子輔吉　　適作鄉行。客裏無伴。僅携心愛之細種金魚三十尾與俱。奈鄉間苦寒。加之雨雪頻仍。氣候究較城市爲冷。雖置之内室。日更井水一次。使其體温不凍僵。無如有翻腮及朝天龍八尾。同時身側不良於游行。視其呼吸亦甚促。少頃。氣反緩而神漸停。四尾竟浮水面死。余頗不忍。然己返魂無香。聽之而己。忽輔吉謂余曰。死馬權作活馬醫。曷不移入温水中。看能甦醒否。余姑如言試之。須臾。居然有生氣。余大樂。復注水入釜中。魚亦遷入。比炭熾。水漸熱。魚亦漸動。視兩腮呼吸亦漸勤。俄竟游動如生。毫無濡滯。指試則水將沸矣。亟易井水。迄今安然無恙。輔吉笑曰。君發明此煑魚重生法。曷不書寄鵑公。余笑應之。筆之爲愛魚者告。

胡天白先生鑒·示悉。紅薇感舊記係一駢體短文·曾刋南社叢刋·（今己散佚無可購取）並無專書·弟鵑敬復·

更正　前日「一得之言」署名「蔡尚思」「思」爲「恩」又「猿染烟癖」之作者爲「儉父」誤爲「傖父」并此更正。

旅歐漫談（二） 131

— 汪亞塵

自羅馬車站開車後約一小時。己到意大利海岸。在車窗遠遠眺望海平綫。只見迷霧間露出了一條白光。四月間意大利天氣。爲年一中最好的時期。天空略帶雲霧。幾隻白鷗在海面覓食。晨間的凉爽。沁人肺腑。這一種暮春柔和的感覺。使旅者精神愉快。一路經海峽無數。人工的點綴。都含美的情調。雖比不上瑞士的優秀。可是也夠得我們贊賞了。午後二時。車停於意大利中部的比閘。pise此問有座斜塔。爲詩人畫家盤桓而不忍去的所在。尤其在美術史上。是極著名的。

在中部意大利。現在我們所看得見的那座卡答鐸拉cathedoral寺院。是建於一零六三年至一零九二年問。大體取basilica式樣。又加上幾分byyantium式的要素。其華麗與雄奇的特色。可稱romanesque建築初期的形式。後來仿照此種式樣的教堂。歐洲各地都能看得到。

在比閘參觀卡答鐸拉教堂。足以使我們滿意。但是還有兩個著名世界的建築物。就是斜塔與洗禮堂。斜塔campanite因歪形。所以沿用其名。一說是建築工事中地盤沉下。故成斜形。還有一說。建此塔時。故意傾斜的。這是一千一百十七年間的建築。全體爲七層洞形。頂上有圓塔。斜度計三十三呎。古色斑爛。其雄偉無與倫比。洗禮堂的雄偉。雖不及斜塔。但其美觀。則勝於斜塔及卡答鐸拉教堂。建於一一五三年。圓形平面。直徑一百二十九呎。純用大理石造成。觀其全體。有簡素的特色。

在比閘遊覽四小時。再乘車前行。同車廂來了一位法國教徒。在羅馬教皇宫充職。人極和藹。教徒講斜塔的故事給我們聽。雖含宗教的意義。却於美術上有密切的關係。歐洲各國。對歷史上的古物。保守得極爲完備。塔雖斜了八百多年。可是没有斜坍。因爲常常有人保管。疊經修理。古意尚存。

銀拆行市開出 135

錢業自上月十九日開業後、表面上雖己營業、而其實在依然半忙半閑之時、無所謂發動與渡充、迨至目前則將漸漸恢復其平時狀態、不過各業尚在停頓、毫無顯赫氣象、因而循仍之、但昨日市面、似稍稍有生機、銀拆己開有市價、形勢略有進展然洋厘則猶在穏站中、

▲銀洋市價及交易（洋厘）早市爲七錢二分三厘一毫二忽半、較前日微好一毫二怱半、做出交易滙劃票欵一百三十萬、鈔票祺塲祇外做開十五萬、銀行交易互市七十五萬、小錢莊交易四十餘萬、客路來源四十餘萬、（銀拆、連日白借無息、始於昨日開有二分行情、形勢稍稍活動、劃頭則仍無加水、錢莊拆票三百餘萬、

紗市驟疲、跌風劇烈、近日變化之速、使人隋入五里霧中、忽升忽降、起伏甚巨、此種狀况、完全受金潮波瀾也、加之商場上流言　起、人心驚惶、至於現紗各帮毫無生氣、而標紗在一百七十七八兩己屬高盤一遇風聲容易變動照事實上論之有上漲之力、然實貨需要不暢、因國内農民購買力不足價格一高、交易愈滯、紗市前途如何、殊難預卜也、

▲市執委會令飭市商會糾正

上海特别市黨部執行委員會、昨訓令上海市商會云、爲令飭事、查各業同業公會、原爲商會會員、商會即爲各同業公會集合組織之法團、如商業上有重要事故、或有特殊問題關係各業全體、須待商議　、應有各同業公會依法請求商會執行委員會討論、其有十分重大、認爲有召集會員代表大會之必要者、亦可依法請求　集、自無庸由各業自行召集同業公會代表大會、轉滋紛歧、乃本月四日、本埠各報刋載、本市各業同業公會、因中央修正同業公會法施行細則第十條條文、特在該商會召集各同業公會代表大會之消息、此種舉動、殊屬不合、亟應加以糾正、且查本市各業同業公會、曾先後聨合組織行規維護委員會、及營業　稅則研究委員會等在法理上均無根據、如果有組織或研究之必要、亦儘可聲請該商會辦理、否則架床疊屋、將來商界意見、難免有淆亂紛歧之處、該商會爲本市商業組織之主體、對於各該同業公會負有指導之責、如有上項抵觸法規之情事發現、亟須隨時加以糾正、爲此令飭該會、即便遵照辦理爲要、切切此令、

▲英領復函之措辭

上海房産公會、昨致英商上海自來水公司函云、逕啓者、准二月十三日惠復、己悉、所有敝會六日函中、述及貴公司要挾舉動、足生反感、與違反貴國對華親善政策各點、未加聲辨、當係認爲係屬不爭之事實之故、惟於水費上再收水費一層、貴公司猶欲繼續將錯就錯、見得不肯思義、敝會殊爲遺　、敝會所希望者、非義之財、貴公司一介不應取諸人、房産主一介不應予諸人、乃今公貴司明知水費上再收水費爲不應有之行爲、然爲保持其繼續取得不當利得之故、以習慣與前洋人住宅百分之四、與華人住宅百分之五、及否則價率增高等三點爲遁詞、更屬不合、數會以爲不良之習慣、應即糾正、房東收取房租、並代收水費其將水費併入而成毛房粗者、原爲便利收取之故、倘便該項水費、由貴公司直接收取、房主自將該項水費除去、乃貴公司利用此　簡便手續、遂至出水費上再收水費之不良習慣、敝會憶及七年以前、貴公司迭變章程、溯及旣往、使房主有械繳小費有三年之多、此亦己成之習慣也、有利於貴公司之習慣、竭盡遵守之能事、而不利於貴公司之習慣、甚至破壞法律、不溯及旣往之原則、而不惜再引證以前華人住宅百分之六洋人住宅百分之五分之往事、此於水費上再收水費之問題、實無關係、然適足以證明貴公司以前、對於華洋住宅待遇不公平之恥辱、又謂如照實在房租計算、價率勢戕增高、敝會以爲事實上應須增高、祗得合法合理、自當承受、然萬不願名低實高、尤不願見人一種金錢、於法於理、均無交付之義務、而被人用强暴脅迫手段攫取而去、不依法主張返還、或且仍繼續繳付者、貴公司謂現行價率、將於本年終止、明年再行考慮、然敝會極不願見貴公司於此數個月之内、繼續用强暴脅迫手段、意圖或實施攫取不當利得也、相應再盡忠告、至希查照共同守法爲荷、

又該會前以自來水交涉事致函英總傾白利南君請其依法制止、該會昨接白領事覆函云、（上略（率二月二十八日大函、爲上海自來水公司、與興平公司、因繳付水價、發　糾紛由、據鄙人所調查、則合同上所稱（實付房租毫無减削）一節、不僅自來水公司、即工部局亦作毛房租解釋、此解釋己奉行四十餘年、並非無理由、又經習慣與時代之默許、貴會會員之反對、似乏有力根據、鄙人未便逕行干涉、方命之歉、相應函達、即希台滄等語、

滬西市民對房捐問題表示 189

▲不願負担兩稅

▲希望根本解决

市財政局對於滬西勞勃生路曹家渡極司非而路周家橋等各越築馬路之商號居户、即將實行征收房捐等情、己紀本報、爰將日來關於該問題之各方情形、探錄於下、

▲市民之表示滬西曹家渡等各號自經市財政局出示佈告、並派員調查房租後、羣情惶恐、咸以各商民等、完全因營業關係、而用工部局之水電及電話、故不得不繳納季捐、凡不用水電及電話之居户、即概不繳納季捐、可見各商號繳納季捐之原因、頗爲明瞭、且際此百物昻貴、營業清淡之時、何堪負担兩稅、兹由德大衣莊等各商號聨名具函市民聨合會第三區分會、請即討論辦法、該分會據函後、特於前晚召集臨時會議、議决先行具函市總會、請求轉向市府申述商民苦衷、務須澈底根本解决後、再行征收、

▲工部局注意自市財政局出示之後、工部局對於此項問題、亦頗注意、近數日間、工部局曾派令華探目數名、前往康腦脫路等處、探詢各商號居民對於市財政局即將實行徴捐之意見、兹悉各商民等均無所表示、大都含糊其詞、以爲滬西範圍甚廣、終須以多數之意見而表决云、

1931.03.07

Internal and External Debt Consolidation Committee 1

Song Ziwen Presents Report

(Nanjing) The Internal and External Debt Consolidation Committee held a meeting at the National Government building at 10:00 AM on the 6th. Chairman Wang Chonghui, committee members Wang Zhengting, Wang Boqun, Sun Ke, Song Ziwen, and Kong Xiangxi attended. Chairman Wang Chonghui presided over the discussions: (1) Song Ziwen presented a report outlining the progress of consolidating internal and external debt in the 18th year, and a proposal for determining consolidation methods. It was resolved to submit the report to the government for review and publication. (2) It was decided to continue the meeting at the National Government building on the 13th. According to a committee member, the internal debt group has not yet been fully established, and the investigation of the external debt group has not been fully submitted. Therefore, the current progress is still focused on reviewing matters. The qualifications for appointing committee members have been determined as: 1. Those related to their official duties; 2. Experts; 3. Representatives from the banking sector. Over thirty people have been appointed and will attend the general assembly. It was also stated that the consolidation of internal and external debt will be conducted on an equal basis, without discrimination. (6th Day Special Dispatch)

Hu's Condition Improved Yesterday 2

Sun Ke and Others Plan to Bring Hu into the City for Recuperation

(Nanjing) Dai Jitao stated that Hu Hanmin felt unwell after arriving at Tangshan. On the 2nd, Hu's daughter, Mulan, went to visit him with a maid. On the 3rd, Deng Zhende, a medical officer from the Ministry of Railways, was invited to provide medical care. Deng went to Tangshan that evening. On the 4th, Deng returned to Nanjing to obtain medication, stating that Hu was suffering from posterior neuralgia, combined with hemorrhoids and gastrointestinal discomfort. On the morning of the 5th, Deng called, saying that Hu had been dizzy the previous night and had a slightly elevated temperature. In the afternoon, Sun Ke and I went to offer our condolences. Chiang Kai-shek sent Liu Ruiheng to examine him. It was found that Hu's temperature and pulse were normal, but his blood pressure was quite high and he needed complete rest and easily digestible nourishment. On the morning of the 6th, Deng returned to Nanjing, saying that he had slept well the previous night and felt better than the previous two days. He ate beef broth and wheat flour and his condition was good. Liu Ruiheng also said that Hu's condition had been improving since the afternoon of the 5th, with a temperature of 99 and a pulse of 80 gradually returning to normal. However, he had slight pain in his head and stomach. His blood pressure was measured at 200, which was likely caused by overwork. A urine test is currently being conducted, but there are no other significant symptoms. He went to examine him again on the morning of the 6th and found nothing unusual, but his blood pressure was too high and he needed long-term rest. (6th Day Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) It is heard that Sun Ke, Kong Xiangxi, and others believe that it is inconvenient to examine Hu Hanmin, who is ill in Tangshan. Sun's private residence behind the Ministry of Railways has fresh air, and they plan to bring Hu into the city for recuperation there. (6th Day Special Dispatch)

Eighth Route Army to Enter Jiangxi 3

Huang Shaoxiong's Trip to Guangxi Undecided

(Hong Kong) The Eighth Route Army plans to fully enter Jiangxi to suppress bandits. Xiang Hanping and Li Yangjing will be the vanguard, and Yu Hanmou and Huang Renhuan will be the reserve. Chen Jitang plans to personally enter Jiangxi to command. Chen left the Yiyang Garden on the afternoon of the 6th to return to the province. It is said that he returned to the garden at 5:00 PM. (6th Day Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Huang Shaoxiong's trip to Guangxi will be determined after Wu Tingyang arrives in Hong Kong and meets with him. (6th Day Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Gu telegraphed the National Government, requesting to resign as Secretary-General, and will go abroad for treatment after recovery. (6th Day Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) The run on Zhongzhi notes has eased. (6th Day Special Dispatch)

Tianjin Aircraft Arrives in Beiping 4

(Beiping) Today, the Tianjin aircraft arrived at Nanyuan at 3:45 PM. Nie Kaiyi said that the Beijing-Beiping test flight was successful. In the future, Beijing-Guangdong flights will also be organized. It is hoped that this will be extended to the Northwest and Xinjiang regions where land and water transportation are inconvenient. Apart from the Zhangbaling and Taishan areas, the Beijing-Beiping route is generally convenient. In the future, when the Beiping-Shanghai route officially opens, newspapers will not be carried in the mail, only letters. Tomorrow, I plan to go to Tianjin to discuss repairing the Tianjin airfield, stay in Tianjin for two days, and return to Beiping. I will take the original aircraft back to Nanjing on the 15th. Tonight, Mobil manager Yuni Gan will host a banquet for Nie. After the Tianjin aircraft arrived, a strong wind blew, fortunately arriving an hour earlier. (6th Day Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Tianjin aircraft flew to Beiping at 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 6th. (6th Day Special Dispatch)

Lijiazhai Station Recovered 5

Brigade Commander Xiang Zhenhua Killed in Action

(Hankou) Military Headquarters reports that the bandit gangs at Lijiazhai have been quelled by various units.

Page 4

and democratic artillery vehicles. The Lijiazhai train station has been completely recovered. The remaining bandits have fled east and west. Military Headquarters has ordered Zhang Yinxiang to personally lead troops north to command the railway artillery to pursue and suppress them. Also, the Bian-Hang Military Headquarters telegraphed that Zhao Guantao has led Wang's brigade south from Xinyang to join forces with Zhang, and traffic on the Beijing-Hankou Railway can be restored within days. (6th Day Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Yuan Ying, commander of the New 12th Division, telegraphed Nanjing, stating that Xiang Zhenhua, brigade commander of the division stationed in Minggang, Xinyang, fought several fierce battles with bandits in the Liulin, Lijiazhai, and Fuzishan areas, killing over 200 bandits and seizing countless spoils of war. He has completely recovered the important station of Lijiazhai, and has dispatched troops to protect railway workers to repair the railway bridges, while tracking down and suppressing the remaining bandits. However, Brigade Commander Xiang personally led the charge and unfortunately died after being shot. Liu Zongzhi is now in command, and has telegraphed headquarters for preferential treatment for his family. (6th Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) The train that departed from Beiping South on the Beijing-Hankou Railway on the 4th arrived in Zhumadian yesterday. Because the bandits north of Xinyang have not retreated, the train returned to Beiping. It arrived in Beiping at sunset today. Outsiders mistakenly thought that the Hankou train had arrived. (6th Day Special Dispatch)

Fan Qiguang Resigns from the Position of Director of the CER and is Succeeded by Zou Shangqing 6

(Harbin) Fan Qiguang resigned from the position of Director of the Chinese Eastern Railway (CER) on the 6th, and was succeeded by Zou Shangqing. Zou is currently a member of the Northeast Cultural Society and Zhang Xueliang's confidential secretary. He is scheduled to arrive in Harbin on the 15th to take office. There will be changes in the senior Chinese railway staff of the CER, which will become apparent within days. (6th Day Special Dispatch)

The Success of Indian Non-Violence 33

Non-violent resistance. Its authority is greater than military force. Its suffering inflicted on the other party is greater than any force. Among the methods of non-violent resistance, the boycott is the most powerful. Since India implemented non-violent resistance, the impact on British commerce has been profound. Now that there is an opportunity to repeal it, commerce can be activated. The British Labour Party, the Liberal Party, and the general merchants have expressed satisfaction. Even other parties opposing the government have criticized the government for making excessive concessions. However, in view of the need to maintain commerce, there is no fierce attack. This shows the great effectiveness of the non-violent movement.

Moreover, the impact of the Indian non-violent movement is not only on Britain. Yesterday, the Washington telegram said that the business community was very pleased with the success of the negotiations between the Governor-General of India and Gandhi. It is expected that this good impact will affect American commerce and that it will benefit the American and Mexican silver mining industries. Today, the New York telegram also said that the market silver price has risen by one-quarter and a half compared to yesterday due to the improved situation in India. It is also known that the Indian problem is related to the world's commerce and finance and its impact is swift. The current stagnation of commerce and the decline in silver prices are a common suffering for all countries in the world, and the reasons are complex. What the Indian problem has recovered is very small, but because of the movement of its machine, all aspects, problems, and awakenings of people's hearts related to finance and commerce are moving towards a perfect path. If everything can be solved smoothly, this dangerous and frightening year may turn into a happy and joyful year.

Foreign Important Telegrams

Text of Agreement Between Viceroy and Gandhi Published 57

Non-Violent Resistance Effectively Terminated

Boycott No Longer a Political Tool

New York Silver Market Trends Upward

▲Reuter's dispatch from New Delhi on the 5th. The original text of the agreement between the Viceroy and Gandhi is now officially published in a form of government announcement. In addition to the terms already announced, this announcement also states that, in accordance with the British Prime Minister's permission on January 9th, efforts will be made to enable representatives of the All-India Congress to participate in future discussions on constitutional improvement plans, as planned by the Round Table Conference. It is also stated that the boycott of foreign goods, mostly aimed at British goods to exert pressure for political purposes, has been agreed that the termination of non-violent resistance includes the effective termination of the boycott of British goods, which will no longer be used as a political tool. As for methods of promoting Indian goods in place of non-Indian goods, or methods of suppressing the sale of strong liquor and drugs, except those that do not go beyond the scope permitted by ordinary laws, the use of pickets is not allowed, and if pickets form any infringement anywhere, they must be stopped. Gandhi had advocated a public investigation into the actions of the police during the disturbances, but Gandhi, knowing that this matter has various difficulties or may hinder the restoration of peace, agreed not to insist. Property that has been confiscated will be returned, except to original owners who stubbornly refuse to pay land tax and other taxes. However, if real estate has been sold to third parties, as far as the government is concerned, this transaction cannot be changed, but anyone can seek legal relief. If positions vacated due to self-resignation have been filled, the government will not be able to restore the former person to their original position. However, local governments should consider other resignation cases with a spirit of leniency. Finally, it states that if the All-India Congress cannot fulfill the obligations of this agreement, the government may take any necessary measures to protect the public and maintain law and order.

▲Reuter's dispatch from London on the 5th. The Secretary of State for India, Benn, read out the announcement issued in New Delhi in the House of Commons today, and explained that the effective termination of non-violent resistance means the effective termination of all activities aimed at promoting resistance by various methods, such as resisting land laws, refusing to pay taxes, publishing newspapers to promote the resistance movement, civil and military officials opposing the government, or abandoning their duties.

▲Reuter's dispatch from London on the 6th. The outcome of the talks between the Viceroy and Gandhi is very satisfactory to officials. Although the Conservative Party is not as happy as the Labour and Liberal Parties, most of them have no objection to the agreed-upon measures. Although a few newspapers feel that this agreement is difficult to tolerate, most commentaries are phrased reasonably. The general public's attention is focused on the revocation of the boycott and the impact it will have on British commerce as a result.

▲Associated Press dispatch from New York on the 5th. Silver prices rose in the market today, partly because the situation in India has now taken a turn for the better. Silver closed at 27 and 7/8, a quarter higher than yesterday's closing price.

New Peruvian Government Falls Again 58

Lasts Only Three Days

Cerro Regains Power

▲Reuter's dispatch from New York on the 5th. The new Peruvian government lasted only three days. The provisional government organized by Elias, the former President of the Supreme Court, together with the naval commander and the army chief of staff, has been overthrown. Cerro has now regained power.

British Naval Budget 59

Reduced by £340,000 Compared to Last Year

Japan Plans to Issue Bonds to Relieve Unemployment

▲Reuter's dispatch from London on the 5th. The First Lord of the Admiralty, Alexander, announced today that as a result of the London Naval Treaty, Britain will demolish two battleships of 25,000 tons each, one battlecruiser of 28,500 tons, and will render one battleship of 25,000 tons militarily ineffective. He also announced the naval budget for the next fiscal year, which requires £51,605,000, a reduction of £342,200 compared to last year. The naval program stipulates the construction of three new cruisers, one flotilla leader, eight destroyers, and three submarines. The naval forces will be reduced by 3,400 personnel, leaving a total of 93,650 personnel. From April 1928 to April 1932, over these four years, the personnel will be reduced by 10,000. He also mentioned the loan of materials to the Chinese government for the training of the Chinese navy, and that the Chinese navy will send officers to Britain for on-site training.

▲Reuter's dispatch from Tokyo on the 6th. The government submitted a bill to the House of Representatives requesting approval to issue bonds worth 6 million yuan to relieve workers at arsenals who have lost their jobs due to the conclusion of the London Naval Treaty.

Germany and Austria Sign Commercial Treaty 60

Implementing Economic Cooperation

▲National dispatch from Vienna on the 5th. After the German Foreign Minister Curtius arrived here, he and the Austrian government began negotiating a German-Austrian commercial treaty to replace the existing provisional agreement, in order to place the economic relations between the two countries on a solid foundation.

British Warship Sets Sail for China 61

Arrives in Shanghai on May 5th, then Transfers to Hankou

▲Reuter's dispatch from London on the 6th. The British cruiser HMS Vindictive set sail for China today. It is expected to arrive in Singapore on April 18th, Hong Kong on April 26th, Shanghai on May 5th, and Hankou on May 7th.

Japanese Proletarian Party Congress 62

Commemorates Yamamoto, Passes Resolutions - Clash With Police, Eighty Arrested

British Postmaster General Resigns 63

Education Bill Decided to be Re-presented to the House of Commons

▲Reuter's dispatch from London on the 5th. Postmaster General Hastings Lees-Smith resigned today, writing to the Prime Minister citing poor health as the reason for his resignation. He said that when the Labour Party formed the cabinet, he accepted this position hoping to assist the government as a speaker in the House of Lords, but the government benches in the House of Lords were full of talent and did not need his assistance. He wants to devote himself to free trade and temperance matters, while still remaining affiliated with the Labour Party and working for the party.

▲Reuter's dispatch from London on the 5th. The President of the Board of Education, Trevelyan, decided to resign after his education bill was rejected by the House of Lords. Today, the new President of the Board of Education, Smith, stated in the House of Commons that the government intends to re-present the education bill that was rejected by the House of Lords to the House of Commons, so that the bill can become law in accordance with the Parliament Act. The Parliament Act stipulates that bills passed by the House of Commons can become law after two years, and will not fail permanently due to opposition from the House of Lords.

Thirteenth National Government Meeting 70

▲Establishment of the Guidance and Reorganization Committee for Culture in Peiping

The following matters were discussed: (1) Resolved to establish the Guidance and Reorganization Committee for Culture in Peiping and to promulgate its regulations; (2) Resolved to promulgate the Regulations and Repayment Schedule for the 20th Year of the Republic of China Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Industry Public Bonds; (3) Resolved to amend and promulgate Article 14 of the Supervisory Regulations for Private Public Utility Enterprises; (4) Resolved to promulgate the Implementation Regulations for the Emergency Law on Punishing Crimes Endangering the Republic of China; (5) Resolved to amend and promulgate the Organizational Regulations of the National Assembly Election General Office, adding "This Office shall have several councillors," to be appointed by this Office from senior officials of relevant agencies, as Article 5, and renumbering the remaining articles accordingly; (6) Resolved to specially appoint Zhang Jinghui as President of the Military Advisory Council; (7) Resolved to approve the resignation of Supervisory Committee member Wu Zhongxin from the positions of Committee Member and Commissioner of the Huai River Guidance Committee; (8) Resolved to appoint Xu Zushan as the National Assembly Representative Election Supervisor for Weihaiwei.

Commercial Transportation Meeting Resolves on Freight Rate Standards 71

At the fifth general meeting of the National Commercial Transportation Conference on the afternoon of the 6th, Chen Guangfu, chairman of the Freight Rate Review Committee, reported the results of the committee's review of various cases, summarizing them into five principles for discussion by the general meeting. It was resolved to adopt the review report. The five principles established by the Review Committee are recorded below: (Principle 1) The methods of constructing freight rates on various routes should be standardized in order to implement the principle of unifying freight rates and developing transportation. The following aspects of the construction method should be standardized: A. The ratio of freight rates between different classes on various routes; B. The method of decreasing freight rates with increasing distance on routes with similar distances; C. The ratio between carload freight rates and less-than-carload freight rates. (Principle 2) A. The freight rates for domestically produced coal should be based on the transportation costs of various routes, as well as the minimum possible range of coal production costs and coal sales prices; B. Coal mines operating on the same route should be treated equally, and freight rates should not be reduced due to reciprocal considerations. (Principle 3) The grades of the following ordinary necessities for people's livelihoods should be lightly regulated: A. Coarse grains, agricultural implements, seeds, cotton, and various agricultural products for development; B. Tree seedlings, coal, firewood. (Principle 4) For the sake of developing Chinese manufacturing and promoting the export of local products, the Ministry of Railways should formulate a freight rate protection policy and consult with the Ministries of Industry and Finance to formulate appropriate measures. (Principle 5) In the event of disasters in various domestic regions, freight rates for the export and import of goods or relief supplies, as well as disaster victims, should be specially reduced.

Jiang Guangnai Goes to Jiangxi to Supervise the Army 72

Guangzhou correspondence: Jiang Guangnai, the Commander-in-Chief of the 19th Route Army, recently received repeated telegrams from generals at the front urging him to enter Jiangxi to preside over the supervision of the army and suppress the bandits. At that time, Jiang had not departed because the bandit suppression matters were still awaiting consultation with Chen Jitang upon his return to the province. However, after receiving the date of Chen Jitang's return south, he decided to depart for Jiangxi on March 1st. It was learned that Chen Jitang returned to Guangzhou on the 28th of last month. After Jiang discussed and agreed with Chen on that day, he immediately ordered his subordinates that evening to pack their luggage and ordered the recovering officers and soldiers to prepare. He also asked the Provincial Government to send a letter to Liu Juke, the Director of the Guangshao Railway Bureau, to prepare one parlor car, six third-class cars, and eight baggage cars for use. This morning at 6:00 AM, the Guangshao Railway Bureau had the cars hooked up as requested and waiting at Huangsha Station. Around 7:00 AM, about a thousand recovered soldiers of the unit lined up at the station and boarded the train. The army equipment and luggage were transported by truck and loaded into the baggage cars. It was not completed until 9:20 AM. At 9:50 AM, Jiang, accompanied by his wife and daughter, arrived at the station by car. At this time, the military music played in unison. Jiang and his wife got out of the car, walked onto the platform, and shook hands with the well-wishers. They then went to the stationmaster's office to rest and wait for the train. I paid a visit and had the following conversation with Jiang: (Q) Are you now going to Northern Guangdong, Commander-in-Chief? (A) Yes. (Q) Can you tell me about your itinerary? (A) I will first go to Shaoguan, then take the land route, passing through Nanxiong and Dayu, and go directly to Ganzhou. (Q) How many days do you expect to arrive in Ganzhou? (A) Because there are other matters along the way, the date cannot be determined. (Q) After arriving in Ganzhou, will you go to Xingguo to meet Commander Cai? (A) I will decide when I arrive. (Q) Will you go to Nanchang to meet Director He Yingqin? (A) Not yet decided. (Q) Where are the communist bandits in Jiangxi Province now? (A) The bandit whereabouts are elusive and unpredictable, but they are roughly still in Yudu and other places. (Q) After you arrive in Jiangxi, can you tell me about your bandit suppression measures? (A) I will first concentrate the various units and then launch a general offensive against the bandits. As for the plan, I need to ask Director He for instructions. (Q) In your opinion, how long will it take to eliminate the bandits? (A) Because the bandits are desperately resisting, the time to eliminate them is difficult to fix. However, we will actively plan the encirclement and suppression and hope to accomplish it in the shortest possible time to reassure the people. (Q) Where is Commander Cai now? (A) Still presiding over the Xingguo Command Headquarters. (Q) How many troops are departing with you this morning? (A) About two battalions of recovered soldiers. (Q) How many staff members are traveling with you? (A) About ten staff members, including Staff Officer Wu Dian. (Q) Is Brigade Commander Huang Yanzhen returning to Shaoguan on the same train? (A) Brigade Commander Huang's mission is complete, so he arranged to return to Shaoguan on the train this morning. The conversation ended here. Li Yangjing, Huang Yanzhen, and others were talking to Jiang about important matters, so I excused myself. At 10:20 AM, the special train had arrived at Xicun from Huangsha Station. Jiang, accompanied by Huang Yanzhen, staff members, and guards, boarded the train. At 10:30 AM, the whistle sounded three times, and the train set off. The well-wishers also departed by car. (March 1st)

Zhang Huizan's Coffin Transported from Jiangxi to Hunan 73

▲Thousands of People from Various Agencies and Important Figures Attended the Funeral Procession

Nanchang correspondence: Zhang Huizan, the Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in Jiangxi Province, was martyred in Futian, Ji'an, on January 28th. His head was retrieved from the Ji River, transported to the provincial capital, and placed in a coffin. The Central Government, recognizing the tragic nature of his death, granted him preferential treatment as an Army General and approved a state funeral. The Jiangxi government allocated 10,000 yuan for funeral expenses and held a public memorial service for three days starting on the 1st of this month, which has now been completed. The coffin will be transported back to Hunan today (the 4th) for a state funeral. At around 8:00 AM, those attending the funeral gathered at the funeral home for a memorial service. Then, a seventeen-gun salute was fired to start the procession. The coffin was covered with the Blue Sky, White Sun, and National Emblem flag and carried by thirty-six pallbearers. The procession was very grand, with a military band, memorial banners, and over a thousand wreaths. There were about a hundred wreaths presented by Chairman Chiang, various Central Committee members, Minister He, and Chairman Lu, all of which were extremely beautiful. The procession stretched for about five or six li. Those attending the funeral included Minister He, Military Affairs Supervisor Wang, Chairman Lu, and representatives from various agencies and groups, totaling several thousand people. The coffin departed from the 18th Division headquarters, passed through Yanjiang Road, Zhongshan Road West, followed Xidajie, turned into Minde Road, turned again into Desheng Road, and re-entered Zhongshan Road to enter Mozi Lane. Then, it proceeded along the Huan City Road from Yangjia Factory to the Yanjiang Road railway pier for ships, crossed the river by barge, and was transported by flower car on the Nanxun Road to Hankou. On this day, the entire city flew half-mast, and all agencies had a day off. There were memorial services along the route of the coffin, which was extremely solemn. (March 4th)

Bandit Alarms on the Southern Section of the Pinghan Railway 74

▲Northbound Trains Currently Stop at Guangshui

Hankou correspondence: On the 2nd of this month, over ten thousand bandits were discovered in Lijiazhai, north of Guangshui. Liulin Station was even occupied. After the vigorous suppression by Yuan Ying's unit of the New 12th Division, fierce fighting continued for two days without completely annihilating them. The Pinghan northbound express train was thus forced to return to Hankou. The details are as follows:

▲Liulin Invaded by Bandits: The New 12th Division, originally stationed in the Xinyang-Minggang area, was responsible for guarding the railway. On this day, upon hearing reports of bandits in the area, Brigade Commander Hou Zhenhua led a company of soldiers to Lijiazhai to suppress them. After several hours of fierce fighting, they were surrounded by the bandits due to their overwhelming numbers. The division dispatched another team, and after fighting fiercely all night, the bandit forces did not weaken, so they temporarily retreated to the vicinity of Minggang. Liulin was thus occupied by the bandits. On the 4th, Division Commander Yuan dispatched another battalion, along with a special service battalion, to counterattack the bandits in Liulin. The bandit forces were unable to withstand the attack and began to flee south. The division's office in Hankou has recently received two telegrams from the division's staff department, reporting the battle situation in detail, which are recorded as follows: (Telegram 1) (1) I have just received a telegram from Liu Jiang, the Director of the Bianxing Military Headquarters, stating that the communist bandits are attempting to seize Xinyang and ordering our division and the 6th Division to make proper arrangements and maintain strict defense. (2) I have received a telegram from He Yao, the Director of the Hanxing Military Headquarters, ordering our division to be responsible for suppressing the communist bandits who have infiltrated Lijiazhai. (3) I have dispatched a brigade, a regiment, Li Battalion, and special service engineers to contain Dongshuanghe and suppress the bandits step by step. They are currently engaged in fierce fighting. (4) I have flown the Second Regiment stationed in Minggang today to increase the pain and suppression at the front line, in order to restore traffic as soon as possible. Respectfully reported. (Telegram 2) I have just received a report from Battalion Commander Li Fengwu stating that I was ordered yesterday afternoon to lead my unit from Minggang to provide assistance. I arrived at Dongshuanghe that evening and, at 1:00 AM this morning, led the team in cooperation with the special service battalion to counterattack the Liulin line. After two hours of fierce fighting, the bandit forces were unable to withstand the attack and fled south. The Liulin station was immediately recovered. I immediately tracked and pursued them along the railway line. The bandits continued to resist stubbornly. I encouraged the soldiers to advance bravely, and at 3:00 AM, we reoccupied Fuzishan and other places south of Liulin Station. In addition to reporting by telegram, respectfully reported.

▲Pinghan Traffic Blocked On the afternoon of the 2nd, the special express train from Hankou to Pingjiang was traveling to Guangshui, and as it was nighttime, it was reported that over ten thousand bandits were harassing Lijiazhai, Xindian, and other places, making it impossible to proceed. The train waited at Guangshui for three or four hours, but still did not receive a telegram from Xindian Station to the north. For the safety of passengers, the train returned to Hankou and arrived at Dazhimen Station at 2:00 PM on the 3rd. According to the investigation of the railway bureau, when the bandits arrived, two locomotives at Xindian Station were destroyed by the bandits, and all equipment inside the station was also destroyed. Over forty telegraph poles were broken along the Guangshui-Liulin section of the route, and many rails were destroyed, resulting in losses of approximately 10,000 yuan. Currently, northbound trains on the Pinghan Railway are temporarily stopping at Guangshui as the terminal. (March 4th)

Hunan Provincial Bank to Issue Paper Money 75

▲Decision to Issue Auxiliary Currency Notes Worth 500,000 Yuan

Changsha Correspondence: The Hunan Provincial Bank, established when Lu Diping was the chairman of the provincial government, was allocated 1 million yuan from the provincial treasury as its foundation and had not issued paper money. After He Jian succeeded him, due to the thriving unified tax revenue, another 500,000 yuan was allocated, bringing the bank's total capital to 1.5 million yuan. For the past two years, the bank's business has been quite profitable. However, since Zhang Gui's army captured Changsha last June, the Fourth Route Army, in urgent need of military funds, withdrew 600,000 yuan from the provincial bank's foundation, which has not yet been returned. Furthermore, the communist Peng Dehuai also invaded Changsha on July 27th, and He Jian withdrew all the bank's deposits as military expenses. It is estimated that four-fifths of the bank's capital of 1.5 million yuan was withdrawn by the government, while the remaining one-fifth, because it was deposited with merchants and not yet due, was preserved. After Changsha was recovered last August, the bank did not officially resume operations. For the past half year, it has only been receiving money and not lending it out. Up to now, about 300,000 yuan of the deposits with merchants have been gradually recovered. As for the foundation withdrawn by the government, due to financial difficulties, not a single cent has been returned. Currently, the bank's actual capital is less than 500,000 yuan. Recently, in order to invigorate the market and regulate finance, He Jian decided to issue paper money in the name of the bank. Because the central government restricts provincial banks from issuing banknotes of more than one yuan, it was decided to issue auxiliary currency notes, in denominations of 10 cents, 20 cents, and 50 cents, printed at the Changsha Xiang'e Printing Bureau. The total amount is provisionally set at 500,000 yuan, to be issued in two phases. The first issuance will be 200,000 yuan, fully backed by cash reserves. After establishing credibility, another 300,000 yuan will be issued, secured by guarantee reserves. All the banknotes have been printed and are scheduled to begin circulation on March 10th. The issuance regulations and reserve inspection regulations have been announced. Currently, there are four types of auxiliary currency notes in circulation in the Hunan market: (1) Auxiliary currency notes of the Shanghai Bank of China, (2) Auxiliary currency notes of the Hubei Provincial Bank, (3) Auxiliary currency notes of 10, 20, and 30 cents issued by the Hunan Electric Light Company, and (4) Auxiliary currency notes of 10, 20, and 50 cents issued by the Hunan Hefeng Match Company. The first two types are not numerous, while the latter two types flood the entire province, amounting to about 400,000 yuan. It is reported that the provincial government has decided to order the recall of the auxiliary currency notes issued by the two companies after the Hunan Provincial Bank's auxiliary currency notes are issued, in order to avoid affecting the market. (March 4th)

The "Tianjin" Plane Detained in Jinan 76

▲Right Wing Oil Pipe Leaking

Jinan Correspondence: The China National Aviation Corporation is conducting trial flights between Shanghai and Peiping (Beijing). Nie Kaiyi, supervisor and deputy director of the aviation group of the company, and four others, flew from Xuzhou to Jinan on the "Tianjin" plane on the 2nd. Last night, Zhang Qifang, acting mayor of Tianjin, sent a telegram stating that the Tianjin airport was suitable for landing. Therefore, the "Tianjin" plane decided to fly to Tianjin. Today (the 4th) at 9:30 a.m., it took off from Zhangzhuang Airport and circled over the city for a week before flying north along the Jinpu Railway. Unexpectedly, at 9:50 a.m., it flew back to Zhangzhuang and landed. I happened to be there and visited Nie Kaiyi. According to him, after taking off this morning, the plane climbed to 2,000 feet over the city. The sky was extremely clear. However, after flying over the Yellow River, the air was filled with thick fog, so they descended to 800 feet and continued to fly north, with a slight reduction in speed. When they reached Sangzidian, they suddenly noticed a white ice-like substance on the right wing. When departing from Shanghai, oil leakage had been discovered in the right wing oil pipe, but it did not hinder the flight. However, they dared not take risks at this point, so they flew back to check. It has now been verified that one of the right wing oil pipes has a significant leak. The other two on the left wing are barely passable. However, repairs are necessary before flying. The most difficult thing at the moment is that repairs may not be possible in Jinan. Nie asked me if I knew anyone at the Dahuaishu Railway Factory and asked me to introduce him. I told him about Qin Wenfan, the deputy director of the railway factory. Nie then sent a mechanic, Yu Yongquan (mistakenly reported as Yu Feiquan yesterday), with me to meet Deputy Director Qin. However, there was still no solution, because the oil pipe is made of steel (i.e., aluminum) and requires oxygen welding (i.e., chlorine gas welding). The railway factory only has electric welding, which is useless. Later, Deputy Director Qin introduced the Lu Da Iron Factory, which has oxygen welding, but after inquiring by telephone, it was found that it was broken and could not be used. At this point, repairs were completely hopeless. Nie then telegraphed Tianjin to report the situation and telegraphed Shanghai to request that someone be sent to Jinan with welding equipment for repairs. It is expected that the person sent by the airline will not arrive in Jinan by train until the evening of the 6th. If the repairs are successful, the plane will not be able to fly out until the afternoon of the 7th. This afternoon, Nie, along with the pilot and mechanic, conducted a test flight at Zhangzhuang Airport, plugging the cracked pipes on the right and left wings, leaving only the remaining two pipes to supply oil. After a 15-minute test flight, they landed again. According to Nie, the test flight results were good, but it takes one and a half hours to fly from Jinan to Tianjin. It is still uncertain whether the two pipes can supply enough oil. Another test flight will be conducted tomorrow morning. If they are confident, they will fly to Tianjin. Otherwise, they will have to wait until after the repairs, he said. (March 4th)

Bengbu Merchants and Residents Strike to Protest Rice Levies 77

Bengbu Correspondence: Guards at the Huaiyuan Sailboat Rice Inspection Sub-Bureau shot and wounded boatmen who were petitioning, inciting merchants, industrialists, navigators, and residents here to march in demonstration and petition the authorities, pleading for assistance. Wei Lihuang, commander of the Anhui North Garrison, according to the request of the masses, has already telegraphed the central government yesterday, requesting instructions on how to handle the matter. Although the Huaiyuan and Bengbu Rice Inspection Sub-Bureaus have faced fierce opposition from the people, they continue to detain rice boats and forcibly collect levies. To express their firm opposition, merchants and residents here unanimously went on strike, ceasing business operations from 9:00 a.m. on the 4th, in order to awaken the authorities. That afternoon, dozens of navigators found Cao Bingxiong and Hang Zhaofeng, two officials from the Bengbu Rice Inspection Sub-Bureau, at the Da Dong Hotel and handed them over to the joint military-police inspection office for custody. Zhang Xin, the newly appointed director of the Rice Inspection Sub-Bureau, and all other personnel have fled without a trace. No one is inspecting rice boats or collecting levies at the riverbank. The Bengbu General Chamber of Commerce believes that the town-wide strike has greatly affected commerce. This afternoon at 3:00 p.m., it specially convened a meeting of representatives from the 38 trade guilds at the Salt and Grain Guild to discuss countermeasures. It was decided to organize an Anhui North People's Petition Delegation to oppose illegal rice levies, and Liu Huaxuan, Dong Jingsheng, Xiao Dafu, and others were elected as representatives, scheduled to go to Beijing within days to petition the central government. They will not stop until the goal of abolishing the levies is achieved. The General Chamber of Commerce and the 38 trade guilds sent a telegram to the central government today, requesting that it be stopped. The Bengbu Transport Guild and others also sent a telegram to Chairman Chiang, requesting that he send a senior official nearby to order the abolition of all rice levies along the Huai River to appease public anger. The original telegram from the Chamber of Commerce and the 38 trade guilds to the central government is recorded below: "To Chairman Chiang of the Nanjing National Government, President Chiang of the Executive Yuan, and Minister of Finance Song Jun: The case of the Huaiyuan Rice Inspection Sub-Bureau shooting and wounding merchants and residents has already been reported to Your Excellencies in two telegrams. However, the sub-bureau disregards the law and ignores public opinion, still intercepting merchant ships and forcibly collecting levies. Merchants and residents throughout the city are on the verge of losing their livelihoods, and the situation is perilous. Therefore, starting at 9:00 a.m. today, they have all closed their shops and are quietly awaiting a resolution. However, the Rice Inspection Sub-Bureau dares to defy the central government's clear orders and oppress merchants and residents, inciting public anger and causing a city-wide strike. If the delay continues for too long, the consequences will be too terrible to contemplate. Therefore, we telegrahically inform Your Excellencies, requesting that you quickly send a special commissioner or telegraph to the military commander stationed there to forcibly abolish the rice levies along the Changhuai area, in order to comply with the law and maintain the people's food supply. We await your urgent orders, the Bengbu Chamber of Commerce and the 38 Trade Guilds respectfully kowtow with seals." (March 4th)

Important News 2

E Province Committee Members Fang and Chen Take Office 78

▲He Chengjun and He Qiyang Swear Them In

Hankou Correspondence: Fang Dazhi, Director of the Construction Department of the Hubei Provincial Government, and Committee Member Chen Guangzu, held an oath-taking ceremony at 10:00 a.m. on the 2nd. He Chengjun, swearing-in committee member from the central government and the Executive Yuan, He Qiyang, swearing-in committee member from the National Government, Wu Xingya, Director of the Civil Affairs Department, Zhang Guanshi, Director of the Finance Department, Huang Jianzhong, Director of the Education Department, Liu Wendao, Mayor of Hankou, and others were present. Presided over by He Chengjun, after the ceremony, Fang and Chen read the oath. Then, He Chengjun, the central government's swearing-in committee member, delivered an address, saying: "Today, Director Fang and Committee Member Chen are holding their inauguration ceremony at the same time. I and my brother were ordered by the Central Party Headquarters and the Executive Yuan to administer the oath. Everyone knows the abilities and knowledge of both comrades Fang and Chen. I hope that from now on, they will follow the oath and do things practically. The oath includes several points: loyalty, integrity, and diligence. The 'loyalty' of loyalty is the loyalty of the Three Principles of the People, which is very meaningful. If loyalty is achieved, the other seven will not be difficult to achieve. Government officials who want to be loyal and work hard at their posts must think of ways to eliminate the bandits who have not yet been wiped out, eliminate corruption, and complete the unfinished construction work. Furthermore, for the people's problems of food, clothing, housing, and transportation, if there are any that have not been resolved, one must think of ways to resolve them. If this can be done, one will naturally be diligent and honest, and one will not violate the teachings of the late leader. All political works can be carried out smoothly. Politics is not about saying much, but about doing it. In the future, I hope that both comrades Fang and Chen will follow the oath and work hard." Next, He Qiyang, the swearing-in committee member of the National Government, delivered an address, saying: "Committee Member Chen has participated in the Northern Expedition several times and has recently assisted Chairman He in defeating Tang Shengzhi, Feng Yuxiang and other rebels, and his achievements are well known. Director Fang has served as the director of the Railway Bureau and has both knowledge and experience. In the past, the province's politics did not have any achievements because the provincial government's organization was not sound. There has not been much establishment in construction. Now that the provincial government is sound and Director Fang is fully responsible for construction, I believe that Comrades Fang and Chen will have good performance after taking office." Then, Committee Member Chen Guangzu delivered a reply, saying: "I have been studying in the military, and politics is not my strong point. Now that I have been appointed by the National Government, I will follow all the laws and regulations of the central government and the provincial government, and I will follow Chairman He and the other committee members and work hard." Director Fang's reply said, "I have limited knowledge, and I am deeply worried that I will fail. From now on, I will follow Chairman He and the other committee members and work harder, and I ask all of you present to give me advice at any time." After the ceremony, music was played, photos were taken, and the meeting was dismissed. After the meeting was dismissed, Chairman He immediately telegraphed the Central Executive Yuan to report the swearing-in process. (March 2nd)

Fuzhou Merchants Refuse to Pay Business Tax 79

▲Also Telegraph the Yuan and Departments to Request Tax Rate Reduction

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Minhou Business Tax Bureau is negotiating with various merchant guilds on the matter of agreeing to pay taxes. Most merchant guilds believe that the tax rate set by the Finance Department is too high and does not suit the business conditions. Moreover, the original draft of the tax rules has not been submitted to the Legislative Yuan for review and approval by the Central Political Conference, so it is considered to be illegal. Therefore, Zheng Shou, the representative of the hardware guild, proposed opposition and refused to agree to pay the tax, saying that it must be approved after the guilds have convened a meeting to discuss and revise the tax rules. The implementation of the Fuzhou business tax has therefore fallen into a standstill. However, after Fujian Province abolished through-taxes, it relied on business tax as compensation. Now that the tax cannot be levied, the Finance Department's revenue is extremely strained. The expenses of the various institutions in the provincial capital for February have not yet been settled. Therefore, Director He Gonggan asked the provincial government for instructions on how to proceed. The provincial government stated that the province's business tax was ordered to be implemented by the Executive Yuan, and the collection regulations and implementation rules were formulated in detail according to the guidelines and supplementary measures issued by the Yuan. Since it has been promulgated, it must be implemented. Fujian is the first province to abolish through-taxes, and merchants should share the difficulties and take into account the overall situation. Fuzhou is the provincial capital, and if each guild can resist payment, merchants in other places will surely follow suit, which will greatly affect the financial future. Therefore, it ordered the Finance Department to levy the tax on schedule, no matter what. If anyone dares to advocate resistance, they should be investigated, reported, and dealt with accordingly. After receiving the order, the Finance Department sent a letter to the General Chamber of Commerce, asking it to convene the merchant guilds, earnestly persuade them, and report and pay the taxes on the specified date, without disobedience. Upon hearing this, the guilds also convened a joint meeting at the Commercial Research Institute at 3:00 p.m. on the 2nd to discuss countermeasures. It was decided to first telegraph the administrative and financial departments to request the provincial government and finance department to postpone the levy and to send representatives to Beijing with the business tax regulations promulgated by the provincial government to petition the administrative, legislative, finance, and industrial departments to reduce the tax rate. Currently, the attitudes of officials and merchants are becoming extreme and it will only be resolved by the Yuan and departments. (March 3rd)

Jiangsu Province's Sericulture Improvement Plan 81

▲The Design Committee Decides on Nine Items

In order to improve the sericulture industry, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mines has specially established a Sericulture Design Committee, and invited experts such as Fei Dasheng as members. It also drafted detailed regulations and submitted them to the provincial government for record. It convened meetings of the members at the provincial residence to discuss everything. Three general meetings were held, and the initial plan for the improvement of sericulture in Jiangsu Province was decided on nine items as follows: (1) Concentrate the entire strength of the sericulture industry to achieve overall balanced development. (2) Unify the administrative promotion of sericulture throughout the province to avoid the drawbacks of divergent methods. (3) Unify the varieties of original silkworm seeds to lay the initial foundation for unified cocoon quality. (4) Promote private mulberry seedling cultivation to meet the urgent needs in reality. (5) Cultivate silk cocoon mulberry and seed mulberry separately to facilitate application. (6) Organize a discussion meeting for sericulture supervision offices to improve methods. (7) Eliminate the monopoly of seed vendors. (8) Encourage the Farmers Bank to give preferential treatment to silk-making cooperatives to promote the silk industry. (9) Suggest to the central government to establish a direct export agency for raw silk to save the silk industry from decline.

According to Takahashi, the head of the business office of the merchant ship company, Zhao Daiwen and Zhao Pilian will also come along. There are more than 50 staff members and secretaries in total. The ship is currently preparing everything for Yan. (February 3rd)

Strict Orders to Recover Slaughter Surtax: The county government previously approved Wang Yun'gong's statement that the merchants of the slaughter tax alleged that the business tax was to be changed and levied due to the abolition of the through-taxes, so they only allowed half of the construction surtax to be levied. When the tooth tax and the slaughter tax were issued in January. On the 15th, the provincial order was to continue to handle the tax as before and allocate it for education expenses, which has nothing to do with the abolition of the through-taxes. Yesterday, it specifically notified the tax payers to abide by the established case and pay the full amount, and not to delay the payment under any pretext, so as not to cause inconvenience.

The Hengyi Steamer of Nan Tang Overturned: The case of the Hengyi Steamer of the Taili Company overturning on the 14th of last month near the Nanshui Xian Temple, drowning ten passengers (men and women), was brought to the county court by the relatives of the deceased. Yesterday, the prosecutor's office opened a court to investigate the case. Five people, including Yang Qiaoquan, Yang Boquan, Mi Zhu, and Wang Wenying, arrived from the family members of the deceased. Prosecutor Zhu Zonghai, who was a candidate, ascended the court and signed the order to bring the company manager Yang Xiangqi, the old helmsman Lu Xingsheng, and the treasurer Xiang Sanbao, who were in custody, to the court for interrogation. First, the plaintiffs, the family members of the deceased, were called one by one and asked to give a detailed account of the tragic incident and requested that the crime be punished according to law to clear the snow for the dead. Next, Yang Xiangqi was interrogated. He stated that he was the manager of Taili Company. The company was a joint venture and was divided into six shares. He only accounted for half of the total amount of the shares, which was 1,800 yuan. He did not know anything about the accident of the steamer. The official asked how it was possible to carry more passengers when only twelve passengers were inspected at the time. Yang replied that there were only a dozen people. Six of them were on official business and did not buy tickets. The steamer staff could not stop them. The official asked if the steamer accident was purely caused by overloading passengers. He said that there were only a dozen people. Now, ten bodies have been recovered, and fourteen people have been rescued. Nine people were revived in the kiln, two in the bathroom, and three others escaped. In total, there were twenty-four people, which is more than double the prescribed number. This proves that overloading passengers caused the disaster. Yang lowered his head and said nothing. Next, Xiang Sanbao was interrogated. He stated that a total of 47 tickets were sold on the ship, carrying 47 people. The steamer had been inspected by the customs, but the tow boat was not inspected. Prosecutor Zhu said that if the tow boat was not inspected, it was a private passenger carrier. How could it be allowed to sail without inspecting the tow boat? He replied that this was the right of the old master, and we could not interfere. After that, Lu Xingsheng was interrogated. He replied that he had been working at Yan Dong for more than two years. The official said that you were not experienced and it was no wonder that something went wrong. When asked why there were so many passengers, why not add another tow boat, he replied that since the company started operating, business has been very slow and the old master was unwilling to spend money to hire a boat. At this point, Prosecutor Zhu ordered the family members to return, and Yang Xiangqi, Lu Xingsheng, and Xiang Sanbao were returned to custody to await public prosecution.

Hangzhou 92

Two Kidnappers Executed by Firing Squad: The Zhejiang Provincial Government previously sent the two kidnappers, Xu Abao and Li Aqiu, who were sent by the Special Operations Squad of the Security Team. According to the interrogation, the bandits confessed that on November 21st of last year at 3:00 PM, they, along with the deceased bandit leader Lao Mao and five others, armed with a wooden-cased gun and a Browning pistol, kidnapped two children, Cheng Zhenqing and Cheng Jisheng, in Jiangwan, Paitou, Wukang. The bandits took turns carrying them until midnight, when they arrived at Xu Kaili's house in Xia Liangting, Sixi, Yuhang, claiming to be borrowing the house for lodging. They did not deny anything. Cheng Abao was identified as the one who first entered the house to kidnap them, and Li Aqiu was identified as the one who stood guard with a gun. The evidence was conclusive, and their crimes were unforgivable. In accordance with Article 2 of the Regulations for the Punishment of Kidnappers, they were each sentenced to two death penalties, of which one would be carried out. They were also deprived of their civil rights for life in accordance with the criminal law. Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, the bandits Xu Abao and Li Aqiu were brought out of the Army Prison and handed over to the Special Operations Squad, who escorted them to the scene of the crime and executed them by firing squad.

Jingdezhen 95

Jingdezhen Porcelain Merchants Petition for Exemption from Porcelain Tax: Jingdezhen is famous for its porcelain production.

Commerce has always been prosperous. Although in the past decade, due to the low tax rate, large quantities of foreign porcelain have been imported, it has inevitably been hit hard, but it has not lost its original position. Unfortunately, last year it was captured by Red Bandits three times. Silver, money, and goods were looted, totaling more than 10 million losses. Tens of thousands of workers were forced to go with them. Therefore, after the bandits retreated, the market was desolate and slumped. Although the Chamber of Commerce has urged various kilns to resume operations, it is difficult to see enthusiasm. Not only are the equipment and raw materials destroyed by the bandits, but it is also difficult to recruit the required workers. The kilns that are now back in operation are less than one-tenth of the usual amount. The General Chamber of Commerce, seeing this, convened a meeting last month to discuss post-disaster measures. It was unanimously agreed that the city was bankrupt and deeply traumatized, and that a request to the government to exempt the special tax on porcelain would not be enough to compensate for the losses. Therefore, on the deletion date, a telegram was sent to the Ministry of Finance requesting a three-year tax exemption for relief. At the same time, the National United Association of Porcelain Merchants in Zhen is also carrying out a tax exemption campaign. It is heard that if necessary, merchants will also have to send representatives to Beijing to petition in order to achieve their goals as soon as possible.

Letter

Letter from Villagers of Xinzhuang, Henan 97

Recently, the newspapers have repeatedly reported that the people of our village have engaged in illegal activities, such as selling drugs, possessing firearms, and robbing in all directions, storing the great crimes, and accusing all the people of our village. After reading it, we were shocked. According to the people of this village, 19 are engaged in the slaughtering and leather industries as the main occupation, and the rest rely on farming for a living. The customs have always been simple and honest, and they are thrifty by nature. There is no one who sells poisonous substances, let alone a secret den for making gold pills. Recently, there have been villains seeking revenge, designing to frame us. All the people of our village swear not to admit it. As for saying that the residents of this village are inherently strong, and in this eventful time in Henan Province, they often surround defeated soldiers and order them to hand over their weapons, that there are now several pistols, several rifles, and even machine guns and cannons, it is even more absurd. There were not many residents in this village to begin with. Although there has been an increase over the years, there are now only about 200 households, but the report says more than 3,000 households, which is very inconsistent with the facts. This is one. The Red Spear Society of Henan Province is nominally the Republic of China, but in reality, it is a disguised form of bandits. It has long been known to both Chinese and foreigners. Jing County belongs to Henan Province, and it is no exception. Burning, killing, and looting are commonplace. And surrounding defeated soldiers and ordering them to hand over their weapons is nothing more than what they do. The facts are all there, and the people of the country know it together. The people of our village have always believed in Islam and never participated in any associations. Now, the actions of the Red Spear Society are being attributed to the people of our village. Isn't this a case of mistaken identity? This is two. In short, the people of our village have always been law-abiding and have never engaged in any illegal activities. All the sections in the report are purely false. In addition to informing various newspaper offices to make corrections, we hereby solemnly declare that we hope all sectors will investigate. Respectfully, Bai Yingfu, Mai Facai, Chen Mingxian, Shan Xinyong, Tong Huchen, and Ding Jukui, villagers of Xinzhuang, Bo'ai County, Henan Province.

Special Article

Outline of the Construction Plan for Shaanxi Province in the 20th Year of the Republic of China (Part 5) 98

▲Drafted by the Shaanxi Provincial Government

(E) Grassland Reclamation and Livestock Farm: Investigation of the wasteland on both sides of the Wei River in Caotan Town, Chang'an, extending from Xianyang in the west to Weinan in the east, covers an area of no less than a thousand hectares. In recent years, only over two thousand mu have been reclaimed, and the rest is still wasteland, covered with lush grass, which is a pity. It is planned to establish a reclamation and livestock farm there, selecting the land that can be cultivated to plant five grains, and the remaining land will be used as a pasture to test various livestock and improve their breeds. The estimated initial cost is over 10,000 yuan. (F) Shaanxi North Reclamation Zone: Northern Shaanxi is sparsely populated and in dire need of prosperity. It is proposed to establish a Shaanxi North Reclamation Zone in the Yan'an area, with 100,000 yuan to attract virtuous people from outside to engage in animal husbandry and reclamation. After making profits, it will be gradually expanded to restore the prosperity of the Northern Wei Dynasty.

In addition, it is planned to advocate the compilation and printing of various popular agricultural and forestry books, to be distributed to the people, such as the improvement of cotton planting, the quality of fertilization, and the digging of ditches to store water, treating the fields, and digging wells. Specialists will be assigned to handle each task according to the actual situation in Shaanxi, carefully considering the implementation, and widely publicizing it to achieve significant results.

Seventh, regarding culture, it is planned to first build an exhibition hall in Xi'an, where various machines and agricultural implements from various countries that can be practical for Shaanxi Province will be selected and displayed to serve as models for the people to imitate. In addition, domestic and foreign products will be displayed for comparison and reproduction. The agricultural and industrial products of the province will also be widely collected, classified, and displayed, with explanations of their uses and manufacturing methods to arouse the public's interest in industry. The estimated initial cost is 100,000 yuan, and it will be gradually expanded in the future. Secondly, it is planned to build a meteorological station on Mount Hua, to connect with major meteorological stations in the country. The estimated initial cost is 50,000 yuan, and it will be gradually expanded. Thirdly, it is planned to promote rain gauges in various counties. The instruments will be manufactured by the Construction Department and ordered by the counties.

The above three matters must be carefully planned this year to prepare for implementation. In addition, there are projects that should be restored, one is the Huaqing Park in Lintong County, and the other is the Revolutionary Memorial Park in Xi'an City. Huaqing Park includes the scenic Lishan Hot Springs. It is planned to restore it and build a hotel to provide rest for tourists. The total cost is estimated to be about 100,000 yuan. The Revolutionary Memorial Park has a large area, and it will take time to complete. The planned cost is estimated to be about 50,000 yuan. The above various plans are currently important projects in Shaanxi and are also necessary for the people of Shaanxi to live. In fact, for Shaanxi, which is riddled with holes, there is nothing that does not need to be built. As the saying goes, "To climb high, one must start from the low; to travel far, one must start from the near." Therefore, the 20th year is only the beginning of the implementation of construction in Shaanxi. I dare not make grandiose claims or engage in empty talk that does not benefit the people's livelihood. (End)
