Gaochang Temple Tram Restored Last Night 188

▲ Mayor Zhang Intervenes to Mediate

Following a martial clash between Chinese tram workers and naval aviation artisans, the #4 and #1 tram lines remained halted at the South Railway Station as of 4 PM yesterday and had not yet resumed service. However, all parties desired to prevent the escalation of the disturbance. Therefore, throughout yesterday, discussions and mediation were conducted by various parties, and progress was made. Traffic on the Gaochang Temple section resumed at 8 PM last night. The details of yesterday's mediation are recorded below:

▲ Tram Workers Petition the Tram Workers' Union

At 9 AM yesterday, permanent members Zhu Hanhe, Xu Yusheng, and Jia Renjie were dispatched to the Municipal Government to request an audience with Mayor Zhang. They were met by Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, to whom the representatives conveyed three requests for the Mayor's consideration: 1. Guarantees against future incidents. 2. Punishment of the main perpetrators. 3. Joint issuance of a proclamation by the Social Affairs Bureau and the Public Utilities Bureau. Secretary-General Yu promised to relay the requests and stated that the proclamation by the two bureaus would be issued and enforced. However, the representatives also acknowledged that tram service must resume immediately upon the proclamation's issuance. They then departed, awaiting a resolution.

▲ Mayor Zhang and Others Mediate in the Afternoon. Mayor Zhang Qun specifically summoned Tram Company Manager Lu Bohong, Traffic Director Zhu Shaoqi, Public Utilities Bureau Director Huang Boqiao, and Police Chief Wang Zijing of the Second District to the Municipal Government to discuss solutions. As a result, a decision was made that Mayor Zhang would be responsible for providing guarantees, the company would be represented by Lu Bohong, and the workers would be temporarily guaranteed by the labor union.

▲ Traffic Restored Last Night at 7:30 PM

▲ Police Bureau Chief Chen dispatched two platoons of the Security Team's motorcycle corps, totaling 100 officers, led by Captain Jiang, to the Tram Company. Two police officers were assigned to each tram on the #1 and #4 lines to provide protection. Simultaneously, Police Chief Wang Zijing of the Second District and Inspector Niu led several senior police officers with 100 copies of the proclamation to the company to post at Gaochang Temple and on various trams. Consequently, tram service in the Gaochang Temple area resumed at 8:30 PM last night.

▲ Proclamation of the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau: Proclamation Regarding the Matter of a Proclamation. According to a report from Wang Zijing, Police Chief of the Second District, on the 1st of this month, ticket sellers on the #1 and #4 tram lines of the China General Edison Company had an altercation with workers from the Naval Aircraft Depot over ticket purchases, which resulted in a mass brawl. As a result, the drivers and ticket sellers feared further danger and temporarily suspended tram service from the Shanghai-Hangzhou Station to Gaochang Temple. In light of this, public transportation is of utmost importance. This Bureau has the responsibility to maintain local order. It is not appropriate to allow arbitrary changes to tram routes. The company's employees must be fully protected to facilitate transportation. In addition to ordering the company to quickly restore the original tram routes, the Second District is ordered to increase the number of police and work with the military to provide strict protection. This proclamation is to be widely publicized. If any further instances of mob disturbances are discovered, those involved will be immediately arrested and severely punished. This is imperative. March 6th, Republic of China Year 20, Bureau Chief Chen Xizeng.

Hand Grenade Explosion Injures Four Men and Women 189

▲ Left Behind by the Aviation Team

▲ Unexpected Disaster Yesterday

The Lu Family Garden, located west of Longhua Town on the south side of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, had been the site of the First Naval, Army, and Air Force Seaplane Team during the autumn of the 18th year of the Republic. When the team was ordered to depart last autumn, they left behind a white iron-cased hand grenade in the main room of the garden. At approximately 7:30 AM yesterday, Zhou Jintu (from Suzhou), the garden's caretaker, his wife, Zhou Zhu, his friend Liu Xiaofu, and Zhou's eight-year-old daughter, Gendi, were having breakfast at the same table when, for unknown reasons, the grenade suddenly exploded. Zhou and Liu were both injured in the head, face, hands, and feet, resulting in a bloody mess. Zhou's wife, Zhu, and daughter, Gendi, sustained slightly lighter injuries. Zhao Lianshan, a police officer from the Sixth Station of the local sub-bureau, rushed to the scene upon hearing the explosion. He quickly transported the four injured men and women to the Shanghai Hospital for treatment. He also recovered a blank iron grenade casing in front of the main room and took it back to the station to be submitted to the Municipal Police Bureau for investigation.

Shanghai West Residents Express Opinions on House Tax Issue 190

▲ Unwilling to Bear Double Taxation

▲ Hoping for a Fundamental Solution

The Municipal Finance Bureau will implement the collection of house taxes from businesses and residences along the newly built roads, such as Roberts Road, Caoxi Road, Jessfield Road, and Zhoujiaqiao in Shanghai West. This has been reported in this newspaper. The recent sentiments regarding this issue from various parties are explored below:

▲ Residents' Expression. Since the Municipal Finance Bureau issued a notice and dispatched personnel to investigate rents in various districts such as Caoxi Road in Shanghai West, public sentiment has been anxious. Many merchants and residents believe that they pay quarterly dues to the Municipal Council solely due to business needs and usage of the Municipal Council's water, electricity, and telephone services. Residents who do not use these utilities generally do not pay quarterly dues. The reason why businesses pay quarterly dues is quite clear. Moreover, at a time when prices are high and business is slow, it is unbearable to bear double taxation. Therefore, De Da Clothing Store and other businesses have jointly sent a letter to the Third District branch of the Citizens' Federation, requesting them to discuss solutions immediately. Upon receiving the letter, the branch held an emergency meeting the night before and decided to first write to the Municipal General Assembly, requesting them to convey the grievances of merchants and residents to the Municipal Government. They must thoroughly resolve the issue fundamentally before collecting taxes.

▲ Municipal Council Attention. Since the Municipal Finance Bureau issued the notice, the Municipal Council has also paid close attention to this issue. In recent days, the Municipal Council has dispatched several Chinese detectives to areas such as Connaught Road to inquire about the opinions of businesses and residents regarding the Municipal Finance Bureau's upcoming tax collection. It is understood that most merchants and residents have not expressed any opinion and are mostly vague, believing that the area of Shanghai West is vast and that a decision should ultimately be made based on the opinion of the majority.

China Child Welfare Association Designates April 4th as Children's Day 193

▲ Request Submitted to the National Government to Order National Observance

The China Child Welfare Association is currently focused on social education, aiming to evoke social sympathy and create a strong public opinion in favor of child welfare. Therefore, at the Executive Committee meeting last month, it was proposed to promote the celebration of Children's Day, stating that children are the future masters of the country and the center of cultural transition. All countries, East and West, pay attention to children's welfare, including various facilities and the name of Children's Day. Domestic institutions give speeches on various methods related to children and seek noble entertainment for children on this day. The child welfare cause in our country is still in its early stages. If there is no extremely important expression and extremely broad publicity movement, it will not be enough to attract the attention of social figures, and Children's Day should be held to promote publicity. However, the climate of each country is different, and the date of Children's Day also varies. The United States holds it on the second Sunday of June and also designates the second Sunday of December as the Happiness Day for Poor Children. Japan designates March 3rd as Girls' Day and May 5th as Boys' Day. It is now designated that April 4th is Children's Day, named "April 4th", and it will correspond to the ancient "March 3rd," "May 5th," "July 7th," and "September 9th" and the current "October 10th" National Day festivals, with the names shining together without conflict. In the spring, the climate in both the north and south should be warm, and it is close to Arbor Day, which is in line with the national plan to plant trees and cultivate people. As a result of the discussions, it was fully approved, and a request was submitted to the competent authorities for approval and forwarded to the National Government to order the observance nationwide. A Children's Day Preparatory Committee was also organized to prepare for the celebration. In the blink of an eye, April 4th is approaching. At that time, the Association will surely have a grand event. We will record it here to see what happens later.

City Chamber of Commerce Bids Farewell to Commander of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps 196

▲ Hoping to Spread the Universal Sentiment of the Chinese Toward Concessions The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce held a tea party at 5 PM the day before to bid farewell to Colonel Commandant E.B. Macnaghten of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps on his return home. Guests included Chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Council Macnaghten, Director Brown, Liu Hongzhong, Yuan Ludeng, Director-General Fessenden, Wang Xiaolai, Zheng Chengqing, Hu Yunqiu, and Xu Tonghao. He will soon leave Shanghai. The Chamber, as a local organization, dares to follow the ancient custom of offering parting words, representing the merchants and residents of the city, to express sincere gratitude to the Colonel Commandant. The Shanghai Concession has always been known as a place where people from all five directions live together. People are not uniform. In recent years, commerce has increased many times over, and it has become coveted by bandits. Therefore, the Municipal Council, under these circumstances, suffers from the shortage of police resources. On the one hand, due to the unreasonable regulations from the past, Chinese military and police forces cannot cooperate in sharing the responsibility for maintaining law and order in the Concession. As a last resort, only merchants can unite to defend themselves. Therefore, the organization of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps can be considered a suitable organization for the current Concession system. The Colonel Commandant has served until now, and there are two points that deserve our praise: (1) He is proficient in military affairs and has fulfilled the mission he was assigned. (2) He understands the history of the Chinese militia for many years and its local relationships, and he has given it considerable trust and guidance. However, because of the various complex situations mentioned above in the Shanghai Concession, it is difficult to eradicate bandits, even if the parties concerned do their best. The Colonel Commandant has served in Shanghai for many years, and he must have a deep sense of this feeling. The reason for the difficulty stems from the special organization of the Concession. Therefore, the attitude that your government took toward the Hankou Concession four years ago was the wisest policy, which is also the same psychology that our people have. The Colonel Commandant is returning home this time, and we hope that he will spread the universal sentiment of the Chinese people to your government and people, so that your country's trade with China, especially with Shanghai, will have even more new and improved opportunities. The Chamber presents a small token to express our gratitude and hope, not to make a grand farewell, but as a memento.

Shanghai-Taicang Buses to Stop Selling Tickets in the Afternoon Starting Today 198

The Shanghai-Taicang Long-Distance Bus Company submitted a document to the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities yesterday, stating that, due to the loose roadbed and dangerous driving, the ticket sales hours had been reduced. It has already been reported to your bureau and approved by order No. 1205. Now, due to continuous light rain, the damaged roadbed has been further eroded, and driving is more difficult than before. However, in order to maintain service as much as possible, it is proposed to sell tickets from 7 AM to 12 PM every day starting from March 7th, and to stop selling tickets in the afternoon, only transporting the passengers who have already purchased tickets in the morning. After the weather clears and the road is repaired, normal traffic will resume. In addition to sending personnel to the Fourth Section of your bureau to explain the difficulties, another official document is submitted, requesting your bureau to review and record the case.

Court Investigates Zou Aizhen's House 199

Tang Huixuan, a Doctor of Economics, sued his wife, Zou Aizhen, for adultery with Chen Henwei, but the case was dismissed. Tang was prosecuted by the prosecutor for bigamy and false accusation. The Criminal Court has repeatedly reviewed the case without a conclusion. Yesterday, the Criminal Court suddenly sent court police officers to investigate the style of the houses where Zou Aizhen lived, the layout of the front and rear floors, and the orientation of the doors, in order to verify the case.

Shanghai South Public Bus Accident 200

▲ Tilting to the Left to Give Way to Oncoming Vehicle

▲ Passengers and Ticket Inspector Injured

Public Bus No. 19-2 (Municipal Permit No. 4142) of the Shanghai South Public Bus Company, traveling from Old West Gate to Longhua, was driven by Du Xuedao, a driver on standby No. 14. At 3:25 PM yesterday, while traveling on Zhizaoju Road at the intersection of Kangqu Road, in front of the Hubei Guild Hall, a car suddenly approached head-on. Du immediately braked and swerved to the left to avoid it. Due to the uneven road, the bus tilted to the left and fell to the ground. Eight passengers, including Ma Jinbiao, Sun Tao, Liang Seng, Yang Tuming, Li Shimian, Wang Yiming, Liang Rulin, and Yang Tingfang, were injured by broken glass. Upon learning of the incident, the company quickly sent the injured and the bus to the Southeast Hospital for treatment. As the injuries were not serious, they were bandaged and released from the hospital. However, Xia Xianyi, the ticket inspector No. 16, sustained slightly more serious injuries and was temporarily kept in the hospital for treatment. The driver, Du Xuedao, sent a letter to the Second District Headquarters of the Municipal Police Bureau for investigation and submitted a detailed report of the accident to the Municipal Police Bureau for review.

Bandits Attempt to Kidnap Hou Huayan 201

▲ Police Receive Information and Arrest Four Bandits

Hou Huayan's home in Xujiawan, Shanghai West, was suddenly visited by kidnappers a few days ago, intending to kidnap him. The First Sub-Bureau of the Sixth District learned of the plan and dispatched police to arrest Zhang Songsheng, Li Quanjin, Sheng Zhangfa, and Pan Tugen and sent them to the Public Security Bureau. According to the two suspects, Zhang and Li, they admitted to going to steal, but did not intend to kidnap. Sheng and Pan claimed to be witnesses to the case. They were transferred to the Local Court yesterday and detained together pending trial.

Woman Jumps into the River Due to Economic Hardship 202

One evening the day before, a middle-aged woman boarded a ferry at the Xinguang Pier to cross the river. However, when the ship reached the center of the river, she suddenly jumped into the river and tried to commit suicide. The ferry master, Zhou A'gen, immediately rescued her and sent her to the Water Police Station. The police chief questioned her and learned that her name was Chen Chunchu, 28 years old, from Songjiang, and living at No. 69 Baoxing Lane, Baoshan Road. She said that she was tired of life due to economic hardship. She refused to answer any further questions. The police chief ordered Chinese detective Hu Changqing to investigate. Xu Shousheng, a relative of the woman, was summoned to the police station, signed the paperwork, and took her home. Before leaving, the police chief told Xu to pay close attention to prevent any further accidents.

Robber Fires Gun Out of Fear, but it Doesn't Go Off 203

▲ Wang Yunxiang Has A Close Brush with Death

Wang Xinging, Du Yansheng, Liu Suizhi, and three other police officers from the Second Precinct of the Shenxiangge Police Station of the Nanshi Public Security Bureau, while patrolling Wangyi Ma Lane, caught sight of a young man who seemed flustered. When he saw the police, he tried to flee. The three bravely chased him. Unexpectedly, the young man turned around and pulled out a gun to fire, but a bullet was lodged in the chamber, so it did not fire. He was eventually apprehended, and the gun was seized. He was immediately taken to the station. After Police Chief Xu interrogated him sternly, the suspect confessed his name to be Wang Yunxiang, 37 years old, from Hebei. He had once served as a police officer in this city. He directly admitted to carrying a gun to rob opium at the wharf but failed. He begged for leniency. Police Chief Xu, due to the case involving armed robbery, immediately prepared a document to report to the Headquarters for further action.

Sequel to the Yongqing Lane Robbery 204

▲ Shi Yincai Confesses Accomplices

▲ Stolen Goods Found at Buddhist Monk's Residence

At around 6 PM the night before, the Detective Team Leader Qi Haitian, along with detectives such as Miao Jinhai, busted seven would-be robbers who opened fire and resisted arrest in Yongqing Lane, across from the Siming Guild Hall, Xiaobeimen. Details are noted in this paper. It is now known that Shi Yincai, one of the seven, confessed to having accomplices such as Monk Zhou, Wang A'da, and a bandit surnamed Sun hiding in the Shanghai West area. Squad Leader Lu then ordered the original detectives to go to the 38th workshop of the Zhentai Yarn Factory in Caoxi Road to apprehend suspect Zhou. Many stolen goods were found, as well as a senior colonel's warrant and insignia from the Xu Huaihai Guerilla Suppression Commander. Wang and Sun were arrested at the 20th milk shed in the same area. During the team's interrogation, suspect Zhou confessed that he was from Wuxi and was wearing a Zhongshan suit. He confessed that on November 19th last year, he robbed Sun Heyun's home in Wangyi Ma Lane, Nanshi, and pawned the loot for money. He also confessed to robbing the Huang family, residents of No. 6 Xiangyan Bridge, Zhabei. Suspect Sun confessed to the robbery of the Lu Qiaji fish shop on Danfeng Road. After receiving the confession, Squad Leader Lu ordered them to be temporarily detained, pending further investigation.

Guo Shaofan Missing 207

Guo Shaofan, a partner at the Yuantong Cloth Factory in Yuxing Lane, Shilu Crossing, Dama Road, this city, is usually cautious and gets along well with his colleagues. He has been there for seven or eight years. He went out after dinner on the 27th of last month and has not returned to the store for more than a week. The store initially suspected that he had returned home, so they immediately sent a letter to inquire, and they were informed that he had not returned home either. The store inspected and found that there were no letters left and that the accounts were not in arrears. Now, the store and his family have been searching in all directions.

Cotton Yarn Tax Certificates Regularly Exchanged for Fabric Shipping Permits 208

▲ Implemented on the 9th of this month

Dyed fabrics that have paid the unified cotton yarn tax must be transported and exported tax-free with a shipping permit exchanged for a cotton yarn tax certificate, as reported. Yesterday, a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency inquired about the implementation date and visited Zhu Wenqi, chairman of the Mercerized Cotton Weaving Industry Association. According to him, it has been agreed with the Unified Tax Bureau to implement it next Monday (9th). However, the method is slightly different from the original agreement. When dyeing and weaving factories transport yarn into the factory, they should first exchange the cotton yarn tax certificate for an entry permit. When the finished dyed fabrics are transported and exported, they should then exchange the entry permit for a shipping permit, which is used to declare customs for tax-free export. However, before the entry permit exchange is implemented, the shipping permit will be temporarily exchanged for a cotton yarn tax certificate. The procedures and location for exchanging the shipping permit will still be handled by the Unified Tax Bureau's personnel at the Silk Mercerized Cotton Weaving Industry Association, as originally agreed.

Chamber of Commerce Responds Regarding the Habit of Delayed Orders 209

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter yesterday to the Shanghai Special District Local Court, stating: "Greetings, Upon receiving your letter, regarding the handling of order disputes, Party B claims that completing customs duties after the goods arrive is considered a form of negotiating delay, commonly known as 'playing the quarrel,' while Party A denies this custom. With conflicting accounts, you requested clarification. Upon investigation, according to common practice, orders and deliveries are processed according to the order specifications. The specifications of each trade generally follow the standard order form filed with the British Chamber of Commerce. This dispute is clearly addressed in Articles 2 and 8 of the standard order form, and by referring to both, the matter can be easily resolved. Furthermore, regarding the payment of taxes, Article 3 of the standard order form stipulates that it is the buyer's responsibility, and therefore, in practice, taxes must be paid upon arrival of the goods, and this cannot be used as a basis for refusing to negotiate. Also, the term 'playing the quarrel' is a common term in the business community for general disputes and does not specifically refer to tax payments. On the 26th of last month, at our Chamber's 33rd regular meeting, this investigation report was thoroughly discussed, and it was resolved to attach a copy of the Chamber of Commerce's standard order form and send a factual reply. Accordingly, a copy of the form is enclosed for your reference."

Stamp Duty Should be Affixed When Collecting Land Practice Certificates 210

▲Notice from the Stamp Tax Bureau

The Jiangsu Shanghai Real Estate Stamp Tax Bureau issued a notice yesterday, stating: "Notice is hereby given that, according to the stamp tax regulations, a stamp duty should be affixed to land title deeds for all properties in the Shanghai urban area, as clearly stipulated. Now that the Shanghai Municipal Land Bureau has completed the measurement and announced the results by district, land deeds will be submitted for verification and exchanged for land practice certificates. This is an important document for property ownership and has the same effect as a land deed. All those who have received a land practice certificate should affix a stamp immediately in accordance with the regulations to make it a legal certificate and ensure the protection of property rights. We are concerned that the public may not be fully aware of this, so this notice is issued for clarification. It is important to know that the land practice certificate is crucial to the rights of property owners, and the stamp duty is very low. If you neglect to pay attention or evade taxes and fail to affix the stamp as required, the authorities will not provide protection in the event of future land disputes or lawsuits, which may damage property rights. Property owners are urged to come to this bureau to purchase and affix stamps as soon as they receive their land practice certificates, in order to comply with the law and protect their rights. The bureau has a summary of the regulations on stamp duty application, which can be provided for on-site viewing. Please comply accordingly and do not make mistakes. This notice is hereby issued. March of the 20th year of the Republic of China, Director Song Jiju, Bureau Address: No. 8, Xiansheng Lane, Zhonghua Road, Xiaoximen."

New Maps Produced by the Hydrographic Office 211

The seabed of the Yangtze River downstream from Wusong to Nantong is heavily silted and undergoes drastic changes. In order to facilitate navigation, the Hydrographic Office of the Ministry of the Navy constantly sends ships to survey and produce a new type of map, with the English name (correctnhlan), for reference by the Ministry of the Navy, shipping authorities, and merchant ships. In the past, the Customs authorities produced a type of blueprint, but it lacked longitude and latitude lines and was not very accurate. Since the bureau adopted the proposal of the International Hydrographic Bureau that only one organization can survey and publish nautical charts, and after taking back the authority to do so, all hydrographic charts produced by the bureau have been exceptionally clear.

Special Shipping News 212

▲Changxing Reduces Prices. To facilitate Chinese people traveling to Hong Kong, Changxing Company has cancelled the third-class cabins on the Asia and Russia liners and converted them into large cabins. The fare from Shanghai to Hong Kong has been reduced from US$17.50 to US$10, which is approximately 36-37 yuan cheaper in Shanghai currency than the original price, and is already in effect.

▲Freight to Yang Increases. Recently, approximately 2 million yuan in silver dollars has been shipped from Shanghai to the Yangtze River, and 600,000 to 700,000 yuan has been shipped to Hong Kong. Yesterday, another 150,000 yuan was shipped. Changxing, Dalai, and other companies in this port have raised the price of shipping silver dollars to Hong Kong from yesterday, from the original 2 yuan per thousand yuan to 3 yuan.

▲Hong Kong Goods Increase in Price. Yesterday, Shanghai-bound cargo to Hong Kong, the various postal shipping companies, due to odd silver prices and hidden expense increases, have agreed to increase water foot prices on all items, such as eggs, medicinal materials, raw kernels, cigarettes, and sundries, by two yuan per ton, to be implemented from yesterday. However, goods shipped to Little Luzon will still be charged at the original price.

Qian Chengjun Concurrently Serves as Military Judge of the Garrison Headquarters 213

Qian Chengjun, a judge of the Criminal Division of the District Court, has been appointed by the Ministry to concurrently serve as a military judge of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, but without additional salary, and has already assumed his duties yesterday. In addition, Wu De, a judge of the Yin County Local Court, has been transferred to Shanghai Court as a prosecutor and reported to duty yesterday.

Resolution of the Guang Shengtang Closure Dispute 214

The Guang Shengtang Pharmacy on Kaizier Road, established for 25 years, announced its closure on March 1 due to building renovations. All the workers, including Pan Fusheng, etc., were in a state of anxiety and had no choice but to request assistance from the Pharmacy Workers' Union and forward it to the Social Bureau. Yesterday at 2 PM, the bureau convened a mediation meeting. Fang Chang'an, representing the capital side, and Shen Zhuotang and Chen Kuaitang, representing the labor side, attended. Zhao Zhenhui and Fang Qingjian from the Pharmacy Workers' Union were also present, with Guo Yongxi from the Social Bureau presiding and Wang Zhixin recording. After a long discussion, the capital side agreed and signed three items of termination: (1) The employment relationship between workers Qian Fusheng, Shen Zhuotang, etc., and Guang Shengtang Pharmacy is terminated; (2) Workers' wages will be paid until the end of May, calculated back to the end of February; (3) The Guang Shengtang station will pay 100 yuan in travel expenses to each of the nine workers, to be divided equally. Thus, the labor unrest at the store was resolved.

The domestic dry tobacco industry has been affected by the cigarette industry and has been declining in recent years. In addition, there was a shortage of tobacco leaves last year, and prices rose sharply. The Dry Tobacco Trade Association convened all its members yesterday to discuss rectification methods and agree on a uniform sales price. The plan is to sell all colors of each type (ie, Ziyuqiu and yellow tobacco) at 22 yuan per dan (unit of weight), effective from today. The association will issue a notice to be implemented immediately, and no price reductions are allowed based on order relationships. Weather Report. The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Yangtze River basin and coastal areas are cloudy and cold, with occasional rain or fog in some areas, but the weather is generally gradually clearing. There are strong winds between Ma'an Island and Kyushu, and the northwest wind is picking up along the mountain and coastal areas. Also, in the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this port was 48.2 degrees and the lowest was 41.7 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 45.5 degrees and the lowest was 39.0 degrees. 216
